(24th Special Telegram)

[Nanjing] The Mongolian-Tibetan Affairs Commission plans to send personnel to Sichuan and Xikang to collect relevant materials in order to plan and resolve the pending Kang-Tibetan case and provide a reference for resolving the Kang-Tibetan issue in the future. (24th Special Telegram)

Investigation of Circulation of Foreign Banknotes in the Interior 14

[Nanjing] Regarding countering the increased issuance of banknotes by foreign banks, Shanghai banking circles have expressed their desire for the Ministry of Finance to strictly stop it. It is said that the banking associations throughout the country will jointly send a telegram to take unified action. According to an investigation into the general situation of foreign banks issuing banknotes in our country, the amount is approximately more than five million. 1. In Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, HSBC, Citibank, Mercantile Bank, and American Express are the most numerous. The main circulation areas are Shanghai, Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Suzhou, Changzhou, Wuxi, Hangzhou, and Ningbo. 2. In Hubei and Hunan provinces, HSBC, Mercantile Bank, and Citibank are the most numerous. The main circulation areas are Hankou, Wuchang, Yichang, Changsha, and Changde. 3. In Fujian Province, American Express is the most numerous. The main circulation areas are Fuzhou, Xiamen, and Gulangyu. 4. In Hebei Province, Citibank, Mercantile Bank, Banque Belge pour l'Etranger, HSBC, and Yokohama Specie Bank are the most numerous. The main circulation areas are Beiping, Tianjin, Shijiazhuang, and Tangshan. 5. In Guangdong and Guangxi provinces, Banque de l'Indochine, HSBC, and various Hong Kong foreign banks are numerous. The main circulation areas are Guangzhou, Shantou, Nanning, Wuzhou, and major ports throughout the province. 6. In Yunnan Province, American Express and Banque de l'Indochine are the most numerous. The main circulation area is Kunming. 7. In Shandong Province, Yokohama Specie Bank is the most numerous. The main circulation areas are Qingdao and Jinan. (24th Special Telegram)

Improvement of Issuance Methods for Aviation Lottery Tickets 15

[Nanjing] The Aviation Highway Construction Lottery Tickets have been issued up to the tenth period. Due to the slightly higher ticket price, they have not been sold out as much as possible. It is learned that the lottery ticket office is now planning to improve the past issuance methods, catering to the psychology of the society. Each ticket costs five yuan, divided into ten strips, each strip costing five jiao. The total prize amount is 250,000 yuan, with a drawing once a month. Other second and third prizes will also be reduced by half according to the original amount. These methods are currently under review by the Ministry of Finance and are planned to be implemented in the eleventh period after the tenth period lottery tickets are drawn on March 1st. (24th Special Telegram)

Academic Groups Telegraph Urging the Closure of the International Savings Society 16

[Nanjing] Twenty-two academic groups, including the Chinese Economic Society, issued a telegram on the 23rd regarding the closure of the International Savings Society. The original text reads: "To the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, the Party Headquarters, Governments, Newspapers, Mass Organizations, and Fellow Compatriots throughout the Provinces, Cities, Counties: National savings should have legitimate channels and must not be carried out in a gambling manner. In particular, it is impermissible for foreigners to absorb the hard-earned money of our toiling masses through gambling-style savings within our country. Organizations such as the French International Savings Society in the commercial ports and the interior are truly alarming. How its organization and operating results are, the Chinese government is not allowed to supervise or ask about. Its content is rumored to be full of many loopholes, and there is no way to guess. However, the funds it has absorbed, excluding profits, have amounted to more than 65 million yuan and are currently increasing without end. Exhausting the country's fat to supply foreign merchants is a dangerous situation that does not need to be explained. It has recently been heard that the government has drafted a method for closure and is currently negotiating. By weighing the circumstances and reasoning, the French side should be able to consider the good relations between the two countries, the feelings and interests of our people, and international morality and justice, and accept it impartially. However, during this period, there are still things that our side should pay attention to, that is, the deadline for the closure of the society must be clearly stipulated and strived for the shortest possible time. Moreover, the refund of savings must absolutely not be left to the society to determine its own rules and arbitrarily discount. It must be calculated in full to ensure that depositors do not suffer any losses and to bring the trade relations between China and France into the right track in the future. Similar gambling-type dog racing tracks, etc., should also be abolished together, so that Chinese people have a good impression and friendship with France, then commerce can naturally become more prosperous, and diplomacy can become more benign. At this time when the lottery savings society has not yet closed, it is especially hoped that fellow compatriots who have not yet joined will absolutely not join again. Those who have already joined should not temporarily withdraw alone and let them hold them hostage. They should register separately by province and district, organize a depositors' union, and use the power of the group to assist the government as the backing of negotiations, striving to achieve the goal of recovering all the principal and interest of the savings and then stopping. At this time of national economic hardship, fellow compatriots can only endure hardship, accumulate bit by bit, and engage in legitimate production investments to save themselves. It is absolutely impossible to have a fluke mentality and harbor extravagant thoughts, and it is especially impossible to use the funds of sweat and blood for foreign merchants to take advantage of. We earnestly hope that the government and the people will work together to recover our rights and interests and actively eliminate all its gambling organizations in the future, exchange them for leakage, and cultivate the people's morality. This is indeed the key to saving the country." [Signed] Chinese Economic Society, Chinese Science Society, Central University, Zhongshan University, Nankai University, Shanghai Universities and Colleges Faculty and Staff Union, Jinling University, Ginling Women's Arts and Sciences College, Hunan University, Peiyang Institute of Technology, Fudan University, Soochow University, Jinan University, Zhejiang University, Xiamen University, Shandong University, Soochow University, Chinese Electrical Engineering Society, Statistical Society, Accounting Society. (24th Central News Agency Telegram)

Rural Inspection Team Arrived in Nanchang Yesterday Afternoon 17

[Nanchang] The Jiangxi Rural Inspection Team arrived in the province from Xun on the afternoon of the 24th and stayed at the Shigang Club. Then, they went to the Lizhi Society to respond to Xiong Shiyao's banquet. In the afternoon, they visited the Agricultural Academy and toured Qingyunpu. In the evening, they responded to the invitation of the Municipal Council. The team started from Nanjing with twenty-five people. One person from the Central News Agency joined in the province. They will visit and inspect in the province on the 25th and 26th and leave the province on the 27th. The schedule will be slightly changed. (24th Central News Agency Telegram)

National Disaster Propaganda Team Reports on the Survey of Border Provinces 18

[Nanjing] The National Disaster Propaganda Team returned to Nanjing. The head of the team, Lin Xinmin, said, "From the surveys we have made over the past three years, we feel that all provinces have a common shortcoming in politics, that is, (corruption) has not been completely eradicated. In remote provinces, even county chiefs who are slightly far from the provincial capital want money and do not understand politics. A major case involving human life can result in the plaintiff being judged to have lost the case due to the power of money. A property case can result in statutory evidence being dismissed as waste paper. A certain border case in the past once caused a sensation, but in fact, it was because the adjutant wanted money, which aroused the rebellion of the Yi people, and the foreigners took the opportunity to instigate discord, almost leading to a major national problem. We entered Guizhou via Hunan. Regarding ethnic groups, the Miao people are the most numerous besides the Han people in each county, divided into raw Miao, cooked Miao, and embroidered ball Miao. The raw Miao and embroidered ball Miao will belong to the uncivilized, only controlled by the Tusi. They support themselves by farming and never enter the city. In terms of education in the province, 99 out of 100 people are illiterate. The climate in Yunnan is very mild, and women still practice foot binding. The Yi people are the most numerous besides the Han people in the province. In places like the Savage Mountain, there is still a type of the most undeveloped savages, who live under the cliffs and cliffs, and their buttocks still have the same tail as apes and monkeys. The educational situation in the province is the same as that in Guizhou. When we returned to Nanjing, we passed through the Annamse coastal defense. There are about 30,000 overseas Chinese living there, and each person must pay the colonial government 30 yuan of head tax every year. The King of Annam, under the control of the French colonial government, leads a carefree life and follows the Chinese Former Qing Dynasty's legacy of opening a department every year to recruit talents, recruiting Xiucai, Juren, Jinshi, and so on." (24th Special Telegram)

Hebei Provincial Government Stipulates Suppression Measures 19

[Tianjin] The provincial government has stipulated suppression measures due to the rampant bandits in various counties. The first step is to send troops to suppress them, and the second step is to have the security regiments handle the clearing of the countryside. It has ordered the counties in eastern Tianjin to actively carry out the work and complete it within February to prevent the bandits from becoming more powerful after the green gauze tent rises and harming the local area. (24th Central News Agency Telegram)

Current Commentary

Review of New Business Policies of Shanghai Money Shops 20

— Yan

The leaders of the money shop industry in this city, recognizing the inadequacy of past business policies to control the current difficult situation, convened a temporary meeting at the Nei Yuan on the 16th. They engaged in a thorough discussion of the present economic downturn and made decisions regarding new business policies, hoping to improve the environment and stabilize the foundation of the industry. These new business policies consist of three items. (See various newspapers of the 20th.)

(1) Of the collateral loans extended by the Central Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Bank of China to various money shops at the close of the last session, more than five million yuan remains unredeemed on schedule. These collateral loans are typically for a term of two months, after which they must be redeemed or extended. This causes the money shops to be constantly anxious and feel constrained. Therefore, the money shop industry now hopes that the Central Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Bank of China will extend the term to be settled every three months to facilitate circulation.

(2) Notify all money shops that they should not extend credit loans to businesses that purchase foreign goods, especially those that sell luxury goods. This is intended to reduce imports and indirectly reduce the large outflow of silver.

(3) Until the market returns to normal, each money shop should adopt the most cautious attitude in its business operations. It is especially important to be prudent with credit loans for businesses without restrictions to build up strength. At the same time, they should take measures to provide security for depositors from all sectors.

Looking at these three items, the first item concerns the extension of collateral loans. Although the second and third items both belong to changes in lending policies, each has its own reasons and effects. Please explain them separately.

(1) Before the closing of accounts in the 23rd year, four money shops, Rong Kang, Yi Kang, De Chang, and Bao Da Yu, suddenly declared bankruptcy one after another due to insufficient turnover. The impact of this event caused unprecedented tension in both the silver and money industries. If the Central Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Bank of China had not released huge amounts of collateral loans, the panic might have spread even further. It is reported that the total amount of collateral loans was 6,667,000 yuan, with a term of seven days and a daily interest rate of two corners. It was distributed among 24 banks and money shops (including two small banks that also have relationships with the money shop industry). By the date of maturity, most of the money shops were unable to redeem due to the unusually tight money supply, and the extension has continued to this day, with more than five million yuan still outstanding. As a result, the New Year's lending rate for remittances opened at two fen on the red plate (February 8th). In less than two days, it rose to six fen and then to one jiao and one fen. Although it later dropped to one jiao due to the Hua Shang Bank providing some allotments, it has maintained a record of nine fen from the 16th to the present, which is unprecedented compared to the "white loan" of previous years. This phenomenon of apparent looseness but actual tightness is not a good sign for the future of the financial industry. Therefore, a small number of money shops have suggested extending the term for three months to make the market turnover more flexible. It is reported that the Central Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Bank of China are considering accommodating this idea, but there are concerns that the market may not be any better than it is today by the end of April.

(2) As for the notification to all money shops not to extend credit loans to businesses that purchase foreign goods, it seems that there are other intentions behind this as well. What is the reason? It is said that at the time of the bankruptcy of the four money shops, foreign merchants expressed doubts about the "credit of money shop notes." By the time new products were launched in the New Year, it was initially reported that foreign merchants refused to ship goods with long-term money shop notes. Later, it was said that only a small number of money shops could be trusted. All of these things were not entirely groundless rumors. However, from the perspective of the money shop industry, this action by foreign merchants is somewhat harsh. Now that the money shop industry has resolved not to extend credit loans to businesses that purchase foreign goods, it may be a strategy to counter foreign merchants, demonstrating passive resistance and seeking sympathy from various sectors within the country. However, the implementation of this policy must be supported by sound execution methods. There must also be considerable coordination with banks in the same industry to take the same steps in order to achieve practical results. Otherwise, abandoning this and taking that will inevitably fall into the trap of high-sounding rhetoric, leaving excuses for foreigners.

(3) The contraction of lending is one of the most important points of the new policy of money shops. This is related to the lifeline of the rise and fall of industry and commerce. When the news came out, the entire city was alarmed. Although Qin Runqing, the leader of the industry, gave a speech saying, "The business policy of each money shop this year... is because it suffered a great deal last year, so it must be determined based on its own strength. For example, after a serious illness, its diet must be based on whether it can digest it... gradually recover." He also said, "Various external rumors are not credible. The account books sent by each money shop have already begun. The reason why those who have not sent them are not because the money shops are unwilling to send them, but because of their own credit issues," and so on. (See this newspaper on the 21st.) Regarding Qin's speech this time, we seem to need to add a little bit. It is said that the contraction of lending has been a consistent policy of the financial industry, and it is rumored that a small number of money shops are preparing to sit down and pay for expenses and remittance interest for a year, implementing a cessation of lending. Given these facts, how can industry and commerce not fall into stagnation? Although various public organizations have repeatedly gathered to discuss remedies, the problem is ultimately serious. Chinese and foreign financial institutions only allow for the utmost assistance within the possible scope of real estate mortgages.

Moreover, the bankruptcy of these four money shops and the collection of accounts by the four money shops of Yin Tai, Yi Chang, Xin Kang, and Yong Feng are by no means just the individual problems of each shop. They are actually deeply related to the entire money shop industry. Further remedies depend on the self-awareness of the money shop industry itself. Comprehensive planning must be done for the internal organizational reforms and the concentration of financial and human resources in order to hope for the revitalization of the front lines. If they continue to be complacent, it will probably not be easy to achieve the effect of reversing the decline and reviving the industry.

Franco-Austrian Compromise Reached After Talks in Paris 21

London Proposal Considered Indivisible

Agreement to Conclude Central European Convention Guaranteeing Peace Based on the Principles of the Rome Accords

Austrian Chancellor and Foreign Minister Leave France for London

[London] Since the German government issued an encouraging reply to the Anglo-French communique of February 3, European pacifism has once again made welcome progress today. The Franco-Austrian discussions in Paris have reached a complete compromise. The participants in the meeting were Prime Minister Flandin and Foreign Minister Laval from the French side, and Chancellor Schuschnigg and Foreign Minister Walterberger from the Austrian side. According to a statement issued tonight, "The authorities of the two countries met all morning, followed by the afternoon, and now they have agreed

(1) Both sides recognize the benefit of concluding a Central European Convention in a spirit of complete equality. The principles have recently been determined by France and Italy in talks in Rome.

(2) Both sides welcome the Franco-British compromise and regard this convention as a security factor. Together with other regional conventions, it can form a complete and indivisible guarantee of peace and facilitate the resolution of various outstanding issues."

After their success in Paris, the Austrian Chancellor and Foreign Minister prepared to leave for London that night for their first return visit. The Austrian Chancellor mentioned the long-standing friendship between Britain and Austria, saying that Austria wants and needs peace and the freedom to achieve its complete independence. The Austrians deeply feel that if there is no foreign interference, they will definitely succeed. The Austrian Foreign Minister also made pro-British remarks. (Reuters, 23rd)

Statement Issued

[Paris] The Franco-Austrian talks have now concluded. According to the statement, the ministers of the two countries jointly studied the general political situation in Europe, and paid particular attention to various situations that can develop the confidence of the peoples of Central Europe and enrich the peace of Central Europe. France and Austria agreed to recognize the Franco-Italian Rome Accords, which have confirmed the principles of the Central European Convention. If the countries concerned can sign this convention in a spirit of complete equality, the benefits will be widespread. The recent Anglo-French London Agreement also recognizes the Central European Convention as a safety factor, and together with other regional conventions, it is a tool to guarantee peace and form a whole that is inseparable. This is particularly gratifying.

Economic Cooperation and Cultural Cooperation As for the economic aspect, Austria has already concluded agreements with France and other countries, and the results are good and satisfactory. The statement concludes that France and Austria have agreed to hold negotiations soon in the hope of concluding a cultural agreement. Generally speaking, people commenting on the statement say that the Austrian government not only expressed its approval in principle of the Danube non-interference treaty, but also listed this treaty among various multilateral treaties, considering it "a tool to guarantee peace and form a whole that is inseparable." It can be seen that Austria has completely supported the position of the Anglo-French London Declaration. In addition, the statement mentions the words "spirit of complete equality," which shows that if the negotiations on the Danube Convention can be based on this spirit, its establishment will be easier.

Restoration Issue Not Involved As for the issue of the restoration of the Habsburg royal family in Austria, it was not mentioned in the talks. In short, the exchange of views between France and Austria has resulted in important progress and is beneficial to the cause of European stability. If they can act with sincerity and patience, all difficulties will eventually be overcome. (Havas, 23rd)

Austrian Prime Minister Visits Britain

[Paris] After the Franco-Austrian talks ended today, Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg and Foreign Minister Weithaler presented the Grand Cross of the First Class of Merit of Austria to Prime Minister Flandin and Foreign Minister Laval. In the evening, the Austrian Embassy held a grand banquet, to which important figures from both countries were invited. The Austrian ministers are scheduled to leave for London tomorrow, not only to exchange views on the European situation.

To Explore British Views on Political and Economic Issues Generally speaking, they will raise specific questions to the British authorities to find out what attitude Britain has toward Austrian economic and political issues. In general, it is believed that in terms of economics, the Austrian ministers will ask Britain to invest in building Austrian railways and use the purchase of a large number of British materials as an exchange condition. As for the political aspect, London political figures believe that the Austrian ministers will definitely inquire about Britain's views on the Central European Convention proposed by the Franco-Italian Rome Accords and the thorny issue of the restoration of the Habsburg royal family. Regarding the restoration issue, news from Vienna said that after the restoration is realized, Austria's efforts to unite the country will be easier to succeed. The British government will adopt a completely objective attitude on this, but it is not absolutely hostile, because no treaty prohibits the restoration of the Habsburg royal family. However, in practice, it is better to postpone the issue. In any case, the restoration issue and the Central European Convention are two completely separate matters and should not be confused. This is what we should pay attention to. (Havas, 23rd)

Explaining Domestic and Foreign Policy [Paris] Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg and Foreign Minister Weithaler met with the French press today and explained Austrian domestic and foreign policies. Chancellor Schuschnigg first reviewed Austria's struggles in the economic field since the overthrow of the empire, saying that the late Prime Minister Seipel first advocated the principle of cooperation among all ethnic groups in spirit and economy. Later, the late Prime Minister Dollfuss followed Seipel and maintained contact with the French authorities from beginning to end. "The policy of national connection does not mean melting all nationalities together, so that the nationalities of various countries lose their nature, but also that various countries compete with each other so that civilization progresses day by day. We firmly believe that this policy is of the utmost importance." Schuschnigg then stated that Austria should maintain complete independence both domestically and externally, saying that this is the main condition for guaranteeing peace. He then explained Austria's constitution and administrative reform measures, saying that some people believe that this is Austria's attempt to establish a dictatorial system, which is a fallacy. In fact, Austria only wants to make constitutional life and the legitimate needs of the people mutually compatible. "The Austrian government will not abandon itself and will not tolerate any political activities that deny the basic principles of the country. The maintenance of Austrian independence can only be better done by the new Austria." In conclusion, Schuschnigg stated that Austria's security has been restored by the power of the government. This is not only a material success, but also a great spiritual victory, etc. Then, Foreign Minister Weithaler explained that Austrian policy is dominated by two perspectives: to expand the scope of friendship as much as possible and to cooperate to maintain peace, etc. (Havas)

French Newspapers Comment with Uniform Satisfaction [Paris] The negotiations between the Austrian ministers and the French authorities ended last night, and all newspapers expressed satisfaction and sympathy for Austria. "Le Petit Parisien" said that France and Austria have the same ideas on the European security system. "L'Ere Nouvelle" commented on the issue of the restoration of the Habsburg royal family, saying, "The activities of the restoration party now seem to be a domestic issue specifically related to Austria and have nothing to do with international affairs. Only when the issue of the restoration of the capitals of Austria and Hungary leads to the reorganization of the old Austro-Hungarian Empire and makes the new countries that succeeded the old empire feel threatened can it be regarded as an international issue. However, the organizers of the new Republic of Austria will be able to deal with this danger, which the French government is deeply convinced of," etc. (Havas, 24th)

Simon to Visit Eastern Europe in Early March 22

Entrusted with Mission to Stabilize European Situation

Will Visit Capitals of Germany, Poland, and Russia

[London] Foreign Secretary Simon plans to visit Berlin, Moscow, and Warsaw in early March to hold talks with Germany, Russia, and Poland. Judging from the scope of his proposed talks, this trip will be the most important diplomatic mission since the European War. It is likely that Lord Privy Seal Eden will accompany the Foreign Secretary. They will not only discuss how to consolidate the foundation of European peace to make it more stable than the Treaty of Versailles, but will also consider issues related to the Far East. According to reliable sources obtained by the Associated Press today, Simon's trip has four purposes: (1) To clarify the opinions of Germany, Russia, and Poland on the European security plan in order to devise conditions that the three countries can jointly accept. (2) To ask Hitler to clearly state exactly how much military strength Germany requires and how much military equipment it will implement. (3) At the same time, Britain will also try its best to make France clearly state the same requirements, because France believes that Germany's manpower and industry are better than France's, so it must reserve leeway. (4) Russia's land and air forces have made great progress, which is also the main reason for Germany's request to increase military equipment. Therefore, Simon plans to know to what extent the strength of the Red Army can be reduced in order to make Germany abide by the military equipment treaty. (National Telegram, 23rd)

Italy Actively Implements Colonial Policy and Prepares for War 23

Troops Continue to Be Sent to East Africa

[Rome] Italy is now actively preparing for war and intends to meet Abyssinia on the battlefield. Italian troops are currently continuing to be sent to Italian Somaliland in East Africa. Last night, the Volcania ship carrying 2,000 Italian troops sailed from Naples and arrived in Messina this morning. From there, another 2,000 to 4,000 troops will be loaded to East Africa. In addition to various specialized personnel for war, the ship also carries doctors and staff from various parts of Italy. Massawa, the capital of Italian Eritrea in East Africa, is extremely tense due to Italy's urgent preparations for war. If Italy and Abyssinia declare war, Massawa will be the center of the Italian military's danger. It is built on a coral island in the Red Sea, with a levee of about one mile long connecting to the mainland. (Reuters, 23rd)

[Rome] The Council of State met today and passed several bills to implement the colonial part of the Rome Agreement between Italy and France on January 7. (There are three conventions on colonies: (1) To resolve the status of Italian residents in French Tunisia in Africa. (2) and (3) To stipulate France's concessions on territory in Italian Libya to the south and Somaliland. The Council of State then approved the agreement previously signed by Italy with Britain and Egypt to demarcate the boundary line. Finally, the cultural agreements signed by Italy and Austria-Hungary were also approved by the Council of State. (Havas, 23rd)

[Rome] Mussolini met with Libyan Governor Balbo today and inquired in detail about the Italian colonies in North Africa, such as the spiritual and material conditions of the local people (including Europeans and natives), the agricultural and commercial situation, and the planned reforms in colonial rule. In addition to praising Balbo's work, Mussolini gave various military instructions. Finally, Mussolini ordered the construction of a large road along the Libyan coast to connect the traffic between Egypt and Tunisia. This project is decided to start in the fourteenth year of the fascist government. In addition to sincerely thanking Mussolini for his concern and assistance to the colonies, Balbo stated that the Italians and natives in the colonies are eager for the Prime Minister to visit. (National Telegram, 23rd)

[Paris] Le Journal published a special article today on Italy's management of East Africa, with many photos, to illustrate the work of the fascist rule in the colonies. The newspaper said that Italy's dispatch of troops to East Africa to protect its various construction projects in the colonies is a necessary measure. Italy has spent countless money on reclamation, road construction, water conservancy, and other projects in the Red Sea colonies. The tribes on the border of the Italian colonies are extremely rampant and pose a threat to the lives and property of Italians at any time. In theory, these tribes should be restrained by the Abyssinian government, but in fact, the Abyssinian government does not have this power. Therefore, it is impossible to seek a solution through diplomatic means. (National Telegram, 23rd)

British Mediation

[Rome] Britain is still actively mediating the dispute between the two countries. British Ambassador to Italy Drummond held important consultations with Italian Deputy Foreign Minister Suvich today on this issue. At that time, both sides mentioned the agreement signed by Britain, France, and Italy in 1906 on maintaining the territorial integrity of the Abyssinian Empire. The result is unknown. (Reuters, 23rd)

Negotiations Break Down

Cairo, Egypt According to news from the capital of Abyssinia, Italy and Abyssinia's negotiations on the organization of a mixed committee to determine the neutral zone have broken down due to Italy's opposition to the participation of European Abyssinian officials. Therefore, the current situation is very worrying. (National Telegram, 23rd)

[Rome] The Abyssinian Embassy in Italy has just issued a statement saying that the Abyssinian government has clearly expressed its acceptance of the proposal to demarcate a neutral area near Walwal on the 9th and 12th of this month and has ordered the commander of the garrison in the Gelo-Gubi area to contact the commander of the Italian army in the Walter area to demarcate the boundary of the neutral area. Yesterday, the Italian army commander notified the Abyssinian army commander that he had reported this matter to the government and is now waiting for the reply from the Italian Ministry of Foreign Affairs. (Havas, 23rd)

Transfer to be Handled by Three-Member Committee

[Geneva] According to a statement issued by the Secretariat of the League of Nations today, Baron Aloisi will accompany the members of the Saar Three-Member Committee to Saarbrücken at the end of this month to participate in the ceremony to be held on March 1 to merge the Saar region into Germany. A Tavern in Munich: Birthplace of the National Socialist Party 25

Party Program Drafted Here Fifteen Years Ago

Hitler Holds Special Commemoration

Munich, Germany On February 24, 1920, Hitler drafted the 25 articles of the National Socialist Party program in a hotel here and announced them to his initial followers to abide by together. This was the beginning of the founding of the National Socialist Party. This hotel has historical value. Today marks the 15th anniversary of the announcement of the National Socialist Party program. A commemoration will be held today, and Hitler will deliver a speech in the hotel in the evening. (Havas, 24th)

Chamberlain's Speech Urges All Countries to Support the League of Nations 26

Persevere and Work Hard to Improve, Use, and Repair Its Weaknesses

To Develop It into a Powerful Tool for International Peace

Paraguay Notifies Withdrawal from the League

[London] British Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain gave a speech in Bradford today, urging all countries to support the League of Nations. He said that what Britain is most concerned about is maintaining peace. The main point of the British government's policy is to consolidate and develop the League of Nations with all the means at its disposal so that it becomes an instrument for obtaining international cooperation and the only powerful instrument. People are too easy to speak out and criticize the League of Nations. It is important to know that the way to remedy its weaknesses is not to abandon the League of Nations, but to make persistent efforts to repair its weaknesses and improve its methods of operation. If possible, it should be made a more powerful tool in the future than it has been in the past, etc. (Reuters, 23rd)

Asuncion The government announced today that Paraguay has declared its withdrawal from the League of Nations. Because Paraguay did not accept the League of Nations' mediation of the Chaco War, the League of Nations considered Paraguay an aggressor. Paraguay was greatly angered, which led to this. In addition, the League of Nations' proposal to lift the arms embargo on Bolivia while still prohibiting it for Paraguay is also a major reason for withdrawing from the League of Nations. In a notice sent to the League of Nations by the Paraguayan Foreign Ministry, it was said that the League of Nations regarded Paraguay's reply to the League of Nations' ceasefire as a rejection of the proposal and took decisive measures. In fact, Paraguay had not yet formally decided at that time, but only asked the League of Nations to reconsider some fundamental issues. Moreover, Paraguay has repeatedly requested the League of Nations to conduct a detailed investigation of the responsibility for the war, but the League of Nations has ignored it. Instead, it has lifted the arms embargo on Bolivia, helping Bolivia purchase military supplies. Therefore, Paraguay has no other way but to withdraw from the League of Nations. At the same time, the Paraguayan army has stepped up its attack on the Bolivian army in Villa Montes in the hope of capturing it before the deadline for the ceasefire set by the League of Nations expires tomorrow. (National Telegram, 23rd)

Capital of Paraguay The Paraguayan government has notified League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol that the country has decided to withdraw from the League of Nations. In November last year, the League of Nations Extraordinary Assembly made mediation proposals on the Chaco dispute. Bolivia immediately accepted, while Paraguay consistently rejected them. Therefore, the League of Nations Consultative Committee recently recommended that the previous ban on arms shipments to the Chaco be lifted for Bolivia and only applied to Paraguay as a sanction. This is probably the reason for Paraguay's withdrawal from the League of Nations. (Havas, 23rd)

[Washington] It is generally believed that since Paraguay withdrew from the League of Nations, the United States is prepared to conduct negotiations between Paraguay and Bolivia on the Chaco dispute, but will wait for Paraguay to make a request before conducting negotiations. (Havas, 23rd)

Wang Chonghui Visits Makino 27

Exchanging Opinions on Sino-Japanese Cooperation

Welcome Reception by Various Factions of the House of Representatives

[Tokyo] Dr. Wang Chonghui, who is visiting Japan, visited Interior Minister Makino at his official residence at 10:00 AM today. They engaged in a cordial discussion for an hour and a half regarding Sino-Japanese cooperation, departing at 11:30 AM. (Telegraphic dispatch on the 24th)

[Tokyo] A dinner party was held by various factions of the House of Representatives to welcome Dr. Wang Chonghui at the Marunouchi Industry Club at 9:00 PM today. Attendees from various factions included Sugawara Den, Kanemitsu Tsuneo, Togo Minoru (all from Seiyukai), Matsuda Genji, Nagai Ryutaro (all from Minseito), Yamamichi Joi and Otake Kanichi (both from Kokumin Domei), totaling seventy-five members of parliament. After a welcoming speech by Mr. Sugawara, Minister of Education Matsuda Genji delivered a speech promoting Eastern culture and establishing Eastern peace. Subsequently, the guest of honor, Dr. Wang Chonghui, delivered a speech stating that Sino-Japanese friendship should be based on morality. If only the commonality of script and race is emphasized, it would be difficult to expect genuine friendship. China and Japan should base their friendly relations on the ancient Eastern morality as the foundation. He also expressed his gratitude. Afterwards, opinions were exchanged frankly, and the meeting adjourned at around 7:00 PM. (Telegraphic dispatch on the 24th)

[Tokyo] Wang Chonghui visited various important figures in Japan today to discuss ways to enhance friendship between China and Japan. The Japanese side mostly stated that China should recognize Japan as a true leader, and take this as the starting point for Sino-Japanese cooperation. This afternoon, seventy important Japanese politicians held a tea party to entertain Dr. Wang. Wang delivered an extemporaneous speech, stating that Western civilization is based on the advancement of material interests, while Eastern culture is based on morality. The closeness of China and Japan should be based on Eastern culture. (Reuters dispatch on the 24th)

Fierce Battle Between Northeast Volunteer Army and Japanese Army in Tonghua 28

[Tokyo] According to Japanese military sources, at 9:00 AM on February 22nd, approximately two hundred members of the Volunteer Army engaged in a fierce battle with the Japanese army near Toutaogou, northeast of Tonghua. In this battle, the Japanese army suffered one death and three injuries. Furthermore, a Japanese squad led by Sergeant Yamamoto was attacked by the Volunteer Army near Yongfengzhen on the 19th, resulting in a fierce battle lasting five hours, with one Japanese soldier and one translator killed. (Hualian Electric dispatch on the 24th)

Two Powerful Figures in the Japanese Army Engage in Open and Covert Struggle 30

General Masaki Plots to Overthrow Army Minister Hayashi

Hualian News Agency Tokyo Correspondence: The distribution of power within the Japanese Army is quite complex. Army Minister Hayashi and Inspector General of Military Education General Masaki have long been at odds. General Masaki belongs to the Southwest faction (mainly the Saga clique) and is skilled in conspiracy. After General Araki resigned as Army Minister, many of General Masaki's faction scattered far away. Therefore, they believe that they must take the position of Army Minister in order to save the situation and are plotting to overthrow Army Minister Hayashi. General Masaki is surrounded by many right-wing ronin, so they are mobilized to slander Army Minister Hayashi and Nagata, the Director of the Military Affairs Bureau, and other senior army officials. Moreover, Army Minister Hayashi did not provide economic assistance to the ronin. The right-wing groups, who have been praising the military, since the era of General Araki as Army Minister, also harbor great resentment towards Army Minister Hayashi. In order to achieve his goal of overthrowing Army Minister Hayashi, General Masaki conspired with political parties. In January of this year, Kuwabara Fusanosuke, the Secretary-General of the Seiyukai, secretly met with General Masaki at Nanpoin in Azabu Ward. Shortly thereafter, Mr. Tsugumo of the Seiyukai exposed the 500,000-yen embezzlement case at the Budget Committee of the House of Representatives. On the surface, it seemed to be an attack on Minister of Communications Tokonami, but the materials for the attack were provided by General Masaki's faction. Therefore, the main purpose was to accuse the military of lacking control, leading to the leakage of confidential documents to the outside world, and to force Army Minister Hayashi to resign. Therefore, it was rumored for a time that Army Minister Hayashi would resign in March. The trend of the two powerful figures fighting each other is of great interest.

A Look at the Pamir Plateau: Past and Present 40

Tashkent Correspondence: The Pamir Plateau is known as the "roof of the world." Previously, it was rarely visited, but now Soviet scientists frequently enter the hinterland for exploration. They have discovered rich deposits of silver, tungsten, and gold, and have also learned that crops can be cultivated at altitudes of 4,000 meters. In 1917, the Pamir had a total of 3,768 hectares of cultivated land; in 1934, it increased to 10,200 hectares. Crop yields have increased by one-tenth, and total production has increased from 27,000 poods to 78,000 poods. Threshing machines, harvesters, and other machines have been discovered in the mountains. Farmers in eastern Pamir use tractors to cultivate wasteland. Before the revolution, the people of the area suffered greatly from food shortages, with mulberry cakes being the main food. Now, the area can be self-sufficient in food for at least nine months of the year. In terms of transportation, until 1932, people had to ride horses to various villages and towns in the Pamir, taking a full month. Now, there is a new highway of 750 kilometers between Osh and Khorog. Khorog also has a power plant. Major Soviet cities can now communicate with the Pamir via radio. There is also an air route between Stalinabad and Khorod. Currently, there are 142 schools in the Pamir, with 5,000 students, whereas before the revolution there were only two schools. Khorog has a normal school with 90 students, as well as theaters and cinemas. Local witch doctors have been eliminated and replaced by modern doctors. There is also a sanatorium at an altitude of 2,000 meters. In short, the primitive life of the Pamir has gradually transformed into a healthy and cultured life. (TASS, January 27)

France's Diplomacy and Economy (Paris Correspondence) 67

France's greatest fear is the resurgence of Germany. If Germany truly revives, it will surely seek revenge against France. Over the past year (1934), the Austrian issue in Central Europe has been difficult for France to handle, and Italy and Germany have frequently shown signs of potential rapprochement. Regarding the Mediterranean hegemony and the contention for supremacy in Central Europe, France and Italy are in an irreconcilable situation. Former Foreign Minister Barthou traveled extensively but ultimately lost his life. His work remained unfinished. His successor, Laval, naturally followed the previous policies and expedited them. In other words, he tried to eliminate the rift between France and Italy and complete the encirclement of Germany.

Before the Saar plebiscite, France had put in a lot of effort, but she herself understood that the administrative power over this region could not be held by France, because the majority of the vote would result in its affiliation with Germany. Therefore, on the one hand, France suggested that the price for mining the coal in the Saar region for five years would amount to 900 million francs, and the excavation costs for the two Walrand coal mine entrances located within France would amount to 45 million francs. If the Saar returned to Germany, Germany would have to repay this amount. However, such a huge sum of money is something that impoverished Germany could not bear. Furthermore, before the Saar people's general vote, France had first made preparations for European diplomacy—establishing an understanding with Italy, making concessions to Italy in North African and East African colonies, and ceding nearly 100,000 square miles of territory to ease the conflict between France and Italy. This was truly a clever move. In this way, France won over Italy and eliminated a large part of the German threat. Except for Poland, all the countries surrounding Germany on the European continent were aligned with France. Even the Soviet Union, which was previously very incompatible with France, is now an ally of France. Therefore, in any case, France and the Soviet Union will not diverge on the issue of Germany. However, the infighting between France and Germany, the purchase of the Saar coal mines, and the guarantee of Austrian independence all pose problems. Therefore, rather than saying that the establishment of the Franco-Italian agreement reduced the crisis in the European political situation, it is more appropriate to say that it is preparing for a greater disaster to erupt in the future.

France holds a huge amount of cash, second only to the United States. At the end of November 1934, the cash reserves amounted to 82,097 million francs. However, the financial situation remains very difficult. In 1933, the state treasury's revenues and expenditures could not offset each other, and the shortfall reached 16 billion francs. Such a huge deficit is something that has probably never been heard of in our motherland. In February 1934, the Doumergue national unity cabinet was established. As a result of reorganizing the finances, the budget still had a shortfall of 18.8 billion francs. Since the financial situation has deviated from the norm, its impact on the general public is naturally very severe. Moreover, the French political arena is full of small parties, and no single party can obtain a majority of seats in parliament. Therefore, politics are always constantly fluctuating, and society cannot be stable. The economic instability is particularly obvious.

The economic instability in France is due, on the one hand, to the impact of foreign countries reducing the value of their currencies, resulting in more imports of foreign manufactured goods and the suppression of domestic manufactured goods exports. On the other hand, France, deeply aware of the lessons learned from the excessive issuance of banknotes since the European War, dared not easily implement a policy of currency inflation, so it had to adhere to the gold standard. As a result, wages were reduced, the number of unemployed people increased, and the voices of dissatisfaction from the working class with the current situation permeated everywhere. In rural areas, due to restrictions on imports and increased tariffs, purchasing power declined instead, while the prices of agricultural products fell, causing farmers to live in poverty and feel dissatisfied with the current situation.

France's industrial production (with 1928 as the base year) was still at 83.5 in January of last year, but it fell to 78.0 in June, and further to 74.0 in October. Wholesale prices (with 1913 as the base year, paper currency price index) were 405 in January of last year, but fell to 356 by the end of November, while retail prices fell by 16.4 percent during the same period. Exports decreased by nearly 600 million francs, and imports decreased by almost 600 million francs, which shows the decline of its trade situation. Given France's accumulation of a large amount of cash, it has no choice but to maintain the gold standard. However, maintaining the gold standard puts pressure on the industrial economy, and domestic economic prosperity cannot be stimulated by any means. As a result, the economic crisis deepens, and the gold standard also faces a crisis, which has a considerable adverse impact on its political situation. (January 24, 1935, in Paris)

Northwest Inspection Notes

— Special Correspondent of This Newspaper, Geng Ya

An Overview of the Recent Turmoil in Xinjiang (3) 68

The Hami Mountain Tangle Incident, initiated by the conversion of local hereditary chieftainships into centrally administered districts, served as the trigger for the turmoil. Its leaders were primarily chiefs under the jurisdiction of the Duo Wang Mansion. (1) Hejia Niyazi, who had made a pilgrimage to Mecca (the holy site of Muhammad), held a high position in the religious community. The Tangle people respectfully referred to Hejia as "Aji." He held an unspecified position in the Wang Mansion. (This reporter inquired with Dr. Yao Le about He's past career. Yao replied that he had previously served the old Wangye, but now he has risen to become the vice chairman of the new provincial government.) After the incident broke out, he commanded a large following. (2) Dr. Yao Le, whose original name was Yao Lobasi, was the son of a Xiang man and a Tangle woman. He was proficient in both Tangle and Chinese. He had been to places like Beiping and Hankou. During the incident, he served as the battalion commander of the Sha Wang's Tangle soldiers. He is now the garrison commander of the Hami Township District. He employs a Chinese secretary and changed his name to Yao Le Boshi. He is known to be alert and straightforward. (3) Sima Yi, the treasurer of Sha Wang, has the air of a politician. (4) Other figures included Grand Ahong, Da Er Gua, and Ismail, the company commander of Little Wang Niezi'er.

The incident dragged on for more than a year. The provincial authorities, finding it inconvenient to march through the Tianshan Mountains, feared further escalation. The Tangle side, having witnessed Ma Zhongying's retreat to Gansu, also sought a peaceful resolution. They negotiated a settlement whereby the provincial government would allocate 100 shi of wheat and 40,000 taels of silver to enable the Tangle farmers affected by the famine to return to the mountains for spring planting. In return, the Tangle people would surrender 2,100 firearms to demonstrate their commitment to non-resistance. Later, the provincial authorities handed over all the wheat funds to Hejia Niyazi. (Some say the funds were not fully disbursed.) He only allocated a portion to his own subordinates, leaving Yao Le's troops uncompensated, which triggered internal repercussions among the Tangle people. Ismail even plotted to capture Yao Le and present him to He. He said, "The common enemy has not been eliminated. Why must we turn against each other?" He also could not bear to see his own people harm each other and released Yao without killing him. However, the infighting continued unabated. The provincial army, seeking to exploit the situation, seized the opportunity to encircle and suppress Yao's forces. Other tribes were also willing to surrender their weapons as agreed. Little did they know that when the deadline arrived, not a single gun was handed in, and instead, each tribe reunited with Yao to resist the provincial army. The provincial army, unprepared, suffered heavy losses.

From then on, the Tangle people established contact with the remnants of Ma Zhongying's forces and further planned to attack Shanshan and Qijiaojing. The provincial authorities urgently dispatched Xiong Fayou's regiment, garrisoned in Zhenxi, to move to Qijiaojing. By that time, Shanshan had already fallen to the insurgent Ma Shiming. The Chinese civilians who failed to escape or who had not accompanied the army from Zhenxi mostly suffered a catastrophe. Xiong's regiment then applied the same methods to the Tangle and Hui people they encountered. Subsequently, they retreated to Turpan, unaware that Ma Shiming, Ma Dexiang, and other troops stationed there and in Yanqi had allied with the Tangle people and laid an ambush. Xiong's regiment, unaware, was completely annihilated. This is what is known as the Turpan Rebellion. The provincial authorities, realizing that the war was escalating daily, and Hami was located 1,400 to 1,500 li away, making transportation difficult, supplies inadequate, and the battle lines too long, ordered Li Hairu's division in Hami to withdraw westward in the spring of the 22nd year. First, they joined forces with the Eastern Frontier Army in Dihua to recapture Turpan, and then they were transferred north to garrison Guchengzi, leaving Hami empty.

After Turpan was recaptured, the Tangle people, following the Tianshan Mountains and the Fan Da Ban, suddenly infiltrated Hongmiaozi, which was more than 20 li away from the provincial capital (Dihua). They colluded with the local Tangle people, took the opportunity to encircle the airport, burned two airplanes, and besieged Dihua for three days and nights. This led to the massacres in Nanguan and Xidaqiao. Sheng Shicai, who currently holds an important position in the Xinjiang military and political circles, was recruited into Xinjiang in the 19th year when Jin Shuren deeply felt that military affairs were not his forte. Sheng served as the chief of staff in the governor's office. The following year, he was promoted to chief of general staff. As the Hami Incident expanded, Sheng was appointed as the commander-in-chief of the bandit suppression campaign, presiding over military affairs at the front. By that time, it had been three years. As the provincial capital was in danger, the provincial army concentrated its defenses in the Dihua area. Sheng was ordered to pursue and attack the Tangle people and Ma Shiming's and Ma Dexiang's troops in the Nanshan Mountains. At that time, transportation was cut off, and news was extremely bad. The eastern and northern routes were in a critical situation. Moreover, rumors of Ma Zhongying's main force attacking Xinjiang again were spreading rapidly and were gradually being confirmed. Therefore, Chen Zhong, Tao Mingyue, Zhao Deshou, and other central military investigators claimed that the turmoil in Xinjiang could not be quelled unless Jin Shuren left. They contacted the military and civilians and launched a surprise attack on the major military and political organs and the provincial government in the provincial capital at 1:00 PM on April 12th. Before dusk, they had occupied all the important locations.

Jin Shuren was completely unaware of the situation beforehand. The mutiny broke out suddenly. The provincial government's guards could not resist and fled through the back door of the provincial government, seeking refuge in the First Public Security Bureau, and then to Meng's regiment, the garrison in the west city. He was ordering the Guihua Army artillery unit to come and defend when suddenly artillery shells began to fly in frequently. Upon discovering that they were from the Guihua Army, he retreated in alarm outside the city to Hongshanzuizi, gathered his core troops, and launched a counterattack, but he was still unsuccessful. He retreated to Suilai and then traveled by car to Tacheng. A Russian consul in Tacheng was extremely friendly with Jin and was willing to help Jin return to the province with effective measures. Jin immediately telegraphed Zhang Peiyuan, the reclamation commissioner in Yili, intending to seek assistance. However, Zhang replied in a telegram, saying, "Inviting a wolf into the house could lead to a big mistake. You should quickly come to Yili and make other plans." At the same time, Lu Xiaozu, the former secretary-general of the provincial government and one of Jin's former subordinates (who was also in Tacheng at the time), also strongly dissuaded Jin, saying that "seeking foreign aid for temporary expediency may bring condemnation to future generations." Jin then realized the situation and quietly left Xinjiang through Russian territory, without thinking of making a comeback.

Yao Le Boshi, One of the Central Figures in the Tangle Rebellion 69

The day after the mutiny suddenly broke out, Sheng Shicai, who was fighting in Wulapai (in the Nanshan Mountains, 40 li south of Dihua), was summoned back by Jin by airplane and stopped at "Yipao Chenggong" (a place name) north of the city. Jin requested a face-to-face meeting, but Sheng dared not go. Sheng's attitude then became clear. After Jin left, 38 representatives from all sides and all ethnic groups formed a Provisional Maintenance Committee and elected Liu Wenlong, the director of the Department of Education, as the provisional chairman, Sheng Shicai, the commander-in-chief of the bandit suppression campaign, as the provisional governor, and Zheng Runcheng of the Northeast National Salvation Army as the garrison commander of Dihua. Liu and Sheng jointly issued a notice to appease the people, stating the significance of the mutiny and listing three conditions: (1) protecting the lives and property of the Jin family, (2) protecting the consulates, and (3) protecting the lives and property of people of all ethnic groups and the Guihua Army. People in the new provincial government said that the overthrow of the old government and the establishment of the new government were based on the success of the April 12th mutiny in the 22nd year, and therefore designated that day as "April 12th Revolution Commemoration Day."

Sheng had only been in Xinjiang for three years and was suddenly in command of the military. He claimed that the April 12th mutiny was unexpected, as he was commanding the military at the front and had no knowledge of it beforehand. However, on the eve of the mutiny, he dreamed of Jin wearing a monk's hat and robes, inviting him to sit in a remote room in a mountain village. Jin immediately slammed the door shut and left. When he woke up, he did not understand the meaning at first, but later he realized that the previous dream was not without cause and effect. In previous years, when Yang Zengxin was in charge of Xinjiang, his subordinates cast a bronze statue to celebrate his birthday, with the words "General Yang's Bronze Statue" engraved on it. (Since Yang's supervision of Xinjiang, the military and civilians have all referred to him as General Yang. Even today, the Tangle and Hui people in Hami still refer to him as the old general.) During the unveiling ceremony in the park, Yang himself was in the front row. When he suddenly saw the statue, which was covered with gold leaf, he did not resemble his true face in Lushan. He blurted out, "Is this General Yang? It's General Jin!" As he spoke, he looked back and saw Jin Shuren standing behind him in formal attire. Everyone then spread the rumor that it was a prophecy of future events. This time, the April 12th mutiny was also preceded by Sheng's dream. People in Dihua also liked to compare it with Yang's statue, saying that everything is predestined and that it was a coincidence. (To be continued)

High-Ranking Generals From Various Regions Arrive in Hankou to Meet Chiang 70

Chen Cheng, Yu Xuezhong, and Others Have All Arrived

Hankou Correspondence: Chairman Chiang arrived in Hankou from Jiangxi on the 21st and stayed at the Central Bank. In recent days, he has received Zhang Xueliang, He Chengjun, Zhang Qun, Qian Dajun, Ye Peng, Chen Xizeng, and others, inquiring about the anti-bandit policies and the security situation in Wuhan. He also telegraphed Chen Cheng, the commander of the 18th Army, Yu Xuezhong, the chairman of Hebei Province and commander of the 51st Army, Wan Fulin, the commander of the 53rd Army, Wang Shuchang, the commander of the Pingjin Garrison, and others to come to Hankou. Chen left Jiangxi on the 22nd aboard the Minxing express steamer and arrived in Hankou at 6:00 PM on the 23rd. Yu, Wan, and Wang also arrived at 6:30 PM by special express train from Pingjin, accompanied by Liu Zhe, the former Minister of Education, Miao Chengliu, Guo Xipeng, Huang Xiansheng, and other division commanders. They were all scheduled to meet Chiang on the 24th. Chen Jicheng, He Zhuguo, Wang Yizhe, Hao Mengling, and other division commanders, who were already in Hankou waiting to meet Chiang, remained in Hankou, except for Chen, who had returned to Puqi. As for those who are about to come to Hankou but have not yet arrived, there is Xu Yuanquan. Xu originally planned to fly east on the 23rd, but due to unforeseen circumstances, he first sent his chief of staff, Yang Shaodong, to Hankou to represent him in meeting Chiang and report on military affairs. Xu himself will depart from Shashi within a few days. In addition, Liu Zhi and He Jian, the chairmen of Henan and Hunan provinces, and Yang Hucheng, the pacification director of Shaanxi and Suiyuan, have also been reported to be coming to Hankou. Chairman Chiang's arrival in Hankou this time is with the determination to eliminate the remaining bandits. He will wait for all the generals to arrive, personally instruct them, and attend the enlarged memorial week training at the headquarters on the 25th. All civil officials above the section chief level and military officers above the rank of captain will participate.

Yu Xuezhong, the chairman of the Hebei Provincial Government, gave an interview to reporters, stating, "We have been summoned to Hankou to report on military and political affairs to Chairman Chiang and Vice Commander Zhang, and to request instructions on everything. We do not plan to attend the establishment ceremony of the Wuchang General Headquarters and will return north immediately. Regarding the Luan Dong Incident, it has now come to an end. The security forces in the war zone have been fully organized, totaling 5,000 men. The timing of their entry into the war zone has not yet been determined and is currently under negotiation. The joint office of the various departments and bureaus of the Hebei Provincial Government will be implemented on April 1st. The relocation of the provincial government to Baoding is difficult to schedule at present. Regarding the issue of the boundary demarcation between the province and the city, the Ministry of Internal Affairs of the Executive Yuan has ordered the provincial and municipal governments to consult and demarcate the boundary. After consultation between representatives from both sides, the provincial government advocates maintaining the original boundaries, while the municipal government believes that the urban area should be expanded. Therefore, no decision has yet been made. The issue of establishing a city in Tangshan will be shelved due to insufficient population and failure to meet the conditions for establishing a city." (23rd)

Recent Situation of Bandit Suppression in Eastern Fujian 71

—Shen and Liu's Brigades Have Both Telegraphed Victories—

Fuzhou Correspondence: Wang Jingjiu, the commander of the Fourth Pacification Zone stationed in Fujian, believed that the banditry in Lianjiang and Luoyuan counties along the coast of eastern Fujian, and in Gutian and Nanping counties along the river in northern Fujian, was rampant. He specially dispatched Shen Fazao's brigade and Liu Anqi's brigade to encircle and suppress them separately. According to the reports from Shen and Liu's brigades, the bandit suppression situation is very smooth. The details are recorded below: (1) Shen's brigade telegraphed that, in recent days, they have been supervising the Qingxiang (clearing the villages) in the sixth, seventh, and eighth districts of Lianjiang and Luoyuan counties and handling the Baojia system. A total of more than 200 bandits have been captured. In addition to more than 30 major bandits who were shot dead on the spot and more than 50 who were sent to the county government, the rest were released after being allowed to reform themselves. A total of more than 300 people have voluntarily come forward to seek self-reformation. More than 70 firearms have been seized. Upon investigation, the Wei Geng bandit gang had about 200 firearms. We have captured more than 70 firearms and scattered more than 60. There are now no more than 80 firearms remaining, about two-thirds of the losses. They have fled to the Western Ocean Island and have been tracked and pursued by our troops. (3) Liu's brigade telegraphed that, among the bandit gangs in Nanping and Gutian counties, Wei Jianlong's faction has the greatest strength. They specialize in intercepting passing ships and wooden rafts along the Minjiang River and levying military rations. Troops have been dispatched in recent days to search and advance along the river. The bandits have retreated into the mountains. Our troops have dispatched teams to encircle them. The bandits are in disarray due to the cut-off of food supplies. Yesterday, another company was dispersed by Li's battalion. The false company commander, Yang Ziming, was shot and killed. Peng Ziang, the largest faction entrenched in Shanyang on the border of Gutian, has expressed sincerity to Jia's battalion and requested permission to surrender their weapons and reform themselves, and to be given security guarantees. This has been accepted. There are few remnants of Wei's bandits remaining, and they will be wiped out soon. The Baojia system will be reorganized and a militia will be organized to strengthen local self-defense. As for the Red bandits in eastern Fujian, the factions of Ma Liefeng (i.e., Li Feng) and Feng Pintai are the most powerful. Ma's bandits have been killed by Ma Hongxing's troops of the Third Security Regiment, and more than half of his troops of more than 1,000 have scattered. Feng's bandits have only 600 or so men remaining and have fled to the Pingxi, Hutou, and Wuting areas under the jurisdiction of Shouning County. (February 23rd)

Jinan's Filial Daughter Enters Prison in Place of Her Mother 72

A Teenage Girl's Heartfelt Plea Regarding a Family Property Dispute

Jinan Correspondence: Zhou Hanzhang of Jiyang was accused by his brother's wife of seizing property and forcing a marriage due to a family property dispute. Zhou went out to make a living, causing his wife, Zhou Hao, to be detained in the military law office. His daughter, Zhou Qingzhen, 16 years old, was extremely saddened and voluntarily requested to enter prison in place of her mother. Shi Jingzhou, the director of the military law office, was sympathetic to her filial piety and, given that the case involved a family dispute, today (22nd) specially approved Zhou Hao's release on bail to go home for medical treatment. Her family dispute will be entrusted to Zhou Hanzhang's father for handling. If it still cannot be resolved, the military law office plans to send the case to the court for handling. The details of the incident are recorded as follows:

Zhou's Family History: Qingzhen's father, Hanzhang, and mother, Hao, are from Zhoujialou Village, Jiyang County. The Zhou family is a prominent family with four brothers: Hanting, Hanzhang, Hanjue, and Hanwen. Hanting and Hanjue died early, and Hanwen is still young. Hanting was adopted by his uncle, Yunshan, who lived at No. 94 County East Alley in Jinan City. His wife, Chen, had no children, so they adopted Hanzhang's son, Qingyu, as their son. Hanzhang, seeing that his widowed sister-in-law and young son could not manage the family affairs, managed them on their behalf. His uncle, Yunshan, was in charge of Qingletang, and Hanzhang's brothers were in charge of Changle tang. They had already separated and lived separately for many years. Although he managed the family affairs on behalf of his son, the properties were separate and not mixed. Later, Hanzhang's father, seeing that his children were grown up, advocated that each should establish their own household. Except for Hanting, who was adopted, Hanzhang, Hanwen, Hanjue's wife, Ma, and the elderly couple were separated into four shares, and 120 mu of land were divided equally, with each share receiving 30 mu, which was enough to make a living. Hanting's family inherited his uncle's business and was known to be wealthy, with more than 200 mu of land. In addition to the house in County East Alley, there was also a house in Jinjuxiang. Zhou Chen gave up the house in Jinjuxiang, leaving it to her parents-in-law. She treated Zhou Ma's two daughters and Hanzhang's daughter, Qingzhen, as her own. After the chaos was over, Zhou Ma wanted to go home, but they could not keep her. She took her two daughters straight back to Jiyang and suddenly accused Zhou Hanzhang of seizing property and forcing her to marry in the military law office of the Third Route Headquarters, claiming that her family had not separated and that Hanzhang had seized several qing of land (including Hanting's land), 300,000 yuan in deposits in Shanghai Bank and HSBC Bank, and forced her to remarry. At that time, Zhou Hanzhang had already gone out to make a living and had not been summoned. His wife, Zhou Hao, and daughter, Qingzhen, lived at the home of her mother, Hao Pin, in Zhenying Street. On the 14th of this month, Zhou Ma and her two daughters went to Zhou Hao's house. In the midst of talking and laughing, she secretly had her daughter report to the Public Security Bureau, saying that Zhou Hanzhang's family was hiding military supplies. Soon after, the police arrived and searched, but found nothing. They then sent Zhou Hao to the General Bureau of Public Security, and then transferred her to the military law office for detention, pending investigation.

A Tragedy: Zhou Hao has dropsy and dysentery. After entering prison, her condition worsened. The day after her detention, her daughter, Qingzhen, went to visit her. Zhou Hao was extremely surprised and said, "How did you, a weak little girl, get here?" The girl, who had studied poetry and books, should explain to her mother that she was willing to imitate Han Ti Ying's story and enter prison in place of her mother, asking her mother to go home for medical treatment. Her mother refused, saying, "This is your filial piety, and I am very happy, but it is not allowed by law. Your father has been falsely accused, and since he is not in Jinan, I should attend the hearing on his behalf. How can you, a weak person, replace me? It is absolutely impossible." At that time, the girl had just recovered from measles. Her mother urged her to go home, but the girl refused, and they embraced and cried bitterly. Everyone watching was moved to tears. Finally, the girl obeyed her mother's order and went home. That night, she drafted a memorial and sent it to the military law office, willing to enter prison in place of her mother, so that her mother could go home for treatment. The memorial stated, "According to the government doctor, her condition is not light. Upon hearing this, my heart and soul were torn apart. If she dies as a result, my mother and daughter will be buried underground, and what face will I have to live in this world? Rather than both of us dying, it is better to replace the old with the young."

Mother and Daughter Reunite: After the memorial was submitted, Shi Jingzhou, the director of the military law office, found the wording heartfelt and, given that the case had no basis in fact, approved her release on bail to go home. Today (22nd) morning, Zhou Hao has returned home, and mother and daughter have reunited. However, Zhou Hao's face is yellow and thin, and she is haggard and pitiful. Zhou Chen is very angry about Zhou Ma's false accusation against Zhou Hanzhang and is preparing to appeal. According to reports, the reasons she has provided are: (1) Zhou Hanzhang did not have any military supplies. (2) Hanzhang has no private property. What Zhou Ma pointed to was probably my family property. (3) Hanzhang only had 30 mu of land that he was entitled to inherit and did not seize my family property or Zhou Ma's family property. (4) The Zhou family has lived separately for three generations, and there is evidence of this. Zhou Ma is actually coveting other people's property, so she took this path and was undoubtedly instigated by others. Previously, seeing that I was widowed and living in difficulty, I had intended to divide several dozen mu from my 170 mu of land, but she refused to acknowledge this. I did not expect that she had ulterior motives and would take such action. (22nd)

Suzhou 73

The Anti-Smoking Association Orders Smokers to Quit

The county's Anti-Smoking Committee, in order to give unlicensed smokers a chance to reform themselves, began to accept smokers' voluntary surrenders on the 21st in accordance with provincial orders, and established two rehabilitation centers to allow the smokers who surrendered to enter the centers to quit smoking. Since the start, only a few people have surrendered, less than ten. The county government has now decided to search smokers' homes from today onwards. Anyone who is unlicensed will be ordered to enter the rehabilitation centers to quit smoking.

Wuxi 74

Investigation of Food Transportation by the General Staff

The National Defense Design Committee of the Nanjing General Staff Headquarters has recently dispatched Zhang Wenduo to investigate the food and various transportation conditions in eleven counties including Wujin, Wuxi, Wu County, Jiading, Qingpu, Songjiang, Jinshan, Liuhe, Yizheng, Nantong, and Taixing. They have specifically requested the provincial government to instruct the above counties to provide full assistance and convenience when the said official arrives. Yesterday, Zhang Wenduo arrived in Wuxi from Nanjing to liaise with the county government and the Chamber of Commerce and conduct thorough investigations into the rice and bean storage businesses and shipping industries.

Second Phase of Land Survey in Five Counties

The Land Bureau of Jiangsu Province is organizing a province-wide land survey. The first phase, involving counties such as Wuxi, has been largely completed. The second phase involves eleven counties including Taicang, Shishan, Nantong, and Siyang. It was originally scheduled to start in April this year. However, it is reported that due to the early completion of the first phase counties, the second phase involving five counties, including Taicang, Chuansha, Baoshan, Chongming, and Wujiang, will be started earlier. Currently, a land survey team has been established in Wujiang, and guide wire surveying has been established in Taicang and the other four counties. The provincial bureau issued team emblems a few days ago to ensure credibility. Furthermore, Bureau Chief Zhu Ping stated that as land surveys in various counties are being completed successively, there is a need for many draftsmen and calculators for the preparation of various land maps and registers. Yesterday, he specifically recruited thirty people each for drafting and calculation, with the examination scheduled to be held at the bureau in Sanguantang, Zhenjiang, starting on March 11.

Robbery and Assault in the Eighth District

In the Guojia Township, Changding Bridge area of the Eighth District, the families of Wu Qiaobao, Wu Agen, and Zhu Xiaobao, who are neighbors and engaged in farming, were targeted. It is reported that around 1:00 AM the night before last, more than a dozen bandits suddenly broke into Wu Qiaobao's house, forced the door open, pulled out pistols, silenced the occupants, and ransacked the house. Subsequently, they went to the homes of Wu Agen and Zhu Xiaobao and continued to rob them. The total losses amounted to more than one hundred yuan. Later, Shao Caibao, a neighbor, heard the noise, came out, and sounded the gong to raise the alarm. The villagers came out to catch the bandits, who fled with the stolen goods, firing several shots into the air as a warning. However, Shao Caibao bravely pursued them and was shot in the buttocks by a bandit with a live bullet. He fell to the ground, bleeding profusely. After receiving the alarm, the Third Sub-station directly under the Public Security Bureau went out to pursue the bandits. At dawn, they intercepted a bandit boat near Xizhuang Bridge and found two bullets on the boat. However, the bandits had all escaped without a trace. The bandit boat and bullets were handed over to the County Public Security Bureau for investigation.
