Economic Journal

How to Obtain a Stable Market and Pacify People's Hearts 190

— Liu Tang

Since the end of the year's accounting and the reopening of businesses, the money market has become tight, and lending has contracted, even more so than before. In previous years, interbank lending was practically free during this period, but this year, the opening rate was already two percent, and later gradually rose to over ten percent. Around the Lantern Festival in the lunar calendar, when businesses were submitting reports of past transactions, there were reports of restrictions on the amount of credit and stricter selection of clients than in previous years. This shows that the current financial situation in Shanghai, the cautious and fearful attitude of those in the industry, and the prosperity or decline of the money market are significantly different from the past, which is clearly visible. Without a solution, this year's working capital for industry and commerce will be difficult to turn over, business operations will be difficult, and the period of "final settlement" will be even closer.

Amidst these difficult and distressed voices, the government has established a Financial Advisory Committee to seek solutions and plan for currency system reform without adopting superficial shortcuts or extreme policies, and without shaking public confidence or hindering the construction of economic prospects. On the one hand, it encourages foreign merchants to import silver, granting tax-free certificates upon import for those importing over 500,000 ounces, and exempting them from taxes upon re-export. As for the money industry, there are three points seen in the newspapers: (1) The collateral loans previously issued by the Central Bank of China and the Bank of Communications will be settled every three months to facilitate turnover. (2) Credit loans will not be granted to merchants purchasing foreign goods, especially those selling luxury goods, in order to reduce import surpluses and silver exports. (3) Before the market returns to normal, all businesses should adopt the most cautious attitude, and unlimited credit loans should be handled with utmost care to build up strength, and safe safeguards should be provided for depositors. Although those in the money industry say that the above is "not to be believed," lending must consider the other party's own creditworthiness and act within its means, which is the operating principle of the money industry this year. In terms of organizations, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Bankers' Association, and local associations have discussed (1) how to stabilize the local market and improve the general business environment, and (2) how the financial and industrial and commercial sectors should seek cooperation to overcome difficulties and seek market recovery during this recession. The result of the discussion is to stabilize the current market, pacify people's hearts, and seek mutual assistance and cooperation between the financial and industrial and commercial sectors within the possible range. In addition, in the United States, which is closely related to the silver market, silver advocates have re-emerged after the gold clause ruling, advocating (1) raising the price of silver to the statutory price of $1.29 per ounce, based on which silver certificates are issued, (2) promptly implementing the Treasury Department's procedure for recovering silver, and (3) allowing international debts to be offset by silver. Recently, the price of gold in Shanghai has also fallen below 900 yuan due to various reasons. Future changes are imminent. However, stability cannot be achieved without this change. Therefore, change may well be a sign of stability. Whether it is a blessing or a curse depends on how we plan for ourselves!

The recent outflow of silver has its external causes and existing loopholes, but if general opinions were slightly more cautious, it would not have caused such panic. Since silver became expensive, people have been talking about and focusing on the silver issue. We admire those who care about current affairs, and we do not expect everyone to have the same opinion. The more we discuss, the more precise we become, so we should not be afraid of detailed discussions. However, there must be a premise: to be internally relevant to the national situation and externally responsive to the times. If we simply parrot others, swallow things whole, disregard facts, and fail to observe advantages and disadvantages, then Yuan Shikai also suspended the exchange of banknotes, and Wuhan also centralized cash. What were the results? It is not difficult to recall. However, we must also understand that foreign countries can succeed because they have the ability to do so. We cannot simply transplant everything to China and expect it to work without any obstacles. Foreign countries do not have concessions; the coming and going of foreign warships is not as direct and unhindered as in China, and they are not stationed permanently; the inland river transportation in foreign countries is probably not as long-term operated by foreigners as in China, and there is no way to recover it; the port inspections in foreign countries are definitely not as scattered and chaotic as in China, allowing for easy smuggling; coupled with our own numerous weaknesses, it is truly a hundred holes and thousands of sores, and there is no time to remedy them. Therefore, every reform, if not handled carefully, will create another opportunity for foreign merchants. And the recent "worship of foreigners" mentality is as fanatical as the "contempt for foreigners" mentality thirty years ago. In the past, the problem was too much confidence, and now the problem is too little confidence, which is another case of excess or deficiency. As a result, foreigners' words and actions are regarded as divine, with the idea that "words are the law of the world" and "waiting for a sage for a hundred generations without doubt." However, they do not know that "it should be based on oneself and verified by the people." Therefore, even though the words have not been put into action, they are enough to warn those who have silver and move those who have no goods. Those who load silver and transport it to Hong Kong and other places are not all because silver is expensive, but because they are afraid of the opinions and propositions of the people of the time and dare not keep it. This is not only true for foreign merchants, but also for Chinese merchants who sell large amounts of bonds, buy and store foreign currency in Hong Kong, and hedge against the pound sterling. In name, they are seeking profit, but in their minds, are they not planning for the worst? I have always suspected that general discussions are flawed by recklessness, and that making speeches and declarations is fashionable. Speakers are unintentional, but listeners are warned. In recent years, there have been many lessons of this kind, but people forget them after the event, and the old habits remain. Now, cash has not been centralized, and currency has not been inflated, but lofty arguments are flourishing, and silver has already disappeared without wings, leading to the embarrassing situation in the market last winter. Sometimes it is compared to illness. Expensive gold and cheap silver, or expensive silver and cheap gold coins, are like a temporary cold. Those with strong bodies can resist it, and they are not afraid of the strong霸道 medicine, which is the currency policy of foreigners. What Chinese people suffer from is the temptation of light and beautiful foreign goods for decades. They are addicted to them, exhausting their energy and spirit, and becoming weaker day by day. They still do not know how to restrain themselves and nurture their health, strengthen the foundation and consolidate the origin. They still want to indulge in pleasure and extravagance, just like the prodigal sons of bankrupt families who eat up their entire fortunes. How can they not be exhausted and die suddenly? They want to treat consumption with medicine for a cold, which is useless.

However, there are things that have the power to disrupt the market and hinder finance, which cannot be compared to lofty theories. The most important thing is the speculators in the market. Market speculation is not surprising in itself, but the speculation of these people is alarming and cannot be achieved by ordinary people. They have access to information that ordinary people cannot know, complain about, expect, or utilize. They can find out things in advance and make arrangements in advance. Often, it is called a rumor beforehand, but it is proven to be true afterwards. Therefore, ordinary people regard rumors as not rumors, which makes it easier for rumors to occur in the market. Since the market is long-term shrouded in pseudo-rumors, how can people's hearts be at peace? When the margin system was changed to use customs gold as the settlement price, when silver export taxes were increased and countervailing duties were levied, the government had not made any statements, and newspapers had not reported anything, but some people in the market had already made preparations and taken steps in advance. As expected, they did not exceed the expectations of these people, and they profited from it. How magical is their skill? Moreover, the manipulation of the securities market, at a time of tight money and market unrest, disregards the dangers to the country, the nation, and the economy, and the boldness of speculators in wildly rising and falling prices is truly astonishing. If this is not corrected for a long time, the market will always be under the control of speculative forces. How can it be stable? Therefore, the difficulties and adversities that come are self-inflicted, and there is no need to blame heaven or others. Does the Book of Songs not say, "Seek much happiness for yourself"? Does the proverb not say, "He who tied the bell must untie it"? That is what it means.

Some people think that stabilizing the market depends on flexible turnover and sufficient chips. Why not borrow a foreign debt to make adjustments? They do not know that borrowing debt requires qualifications. With qualifications, all conditions can be cheap. Without such qualifications, it is like a poor person borrowing usurious loans, with harsh conditions and increased principal and interest. Furthermore, the new method of trade now is almost reverting to the ancient times of bartering. The new method of lending also wants to use goods as cash. Therefore, what is borrowed is often goods, and what is repaid is still cash. If what is borrowed is industrial products, it will help them promote their products and create a monopoly market, which is like drinking poison to quench thirst. Even if what is borrowed is cash, but the conditions are harsh, binding, and involve all future rights, it is like "curing the sore in front of you, but cutting out the flesh in your heart." Except for those who intend to make a desperate gamble, I think no one dares to accept it.

If the Shanghai market wants to be stable, (1) it still needs solutions for the rural economy. If the rural economy is prosperous, the city will naturally prosper. However, how to flow funds into the countryside, how the countryside can accept these funds, and how to use these funds are all major issues that cannot be covered in this article. (2) Eliminate the causes of market unrest, namely the real estate issue. Real estate has been regarded as the best investment, and with the manipulation of real estate developers, prices have risen day and night, resulting in prices that are not commensurate with the market environment. In the bustling city, there are often large plots of vacant land waiting to be sold, and vacant houses are lined up, but there are no tenants. If the market is good, real estate can barely maintain the status quo. Unfortunately, it also coincided with last year's market situation. Foreign banks transported their silver deposits overseas, and they did not want to renew their collateral loans. Chinese banks saw the situation and tried to protect themselves, and they did not dare to bear too much. The once-popular real estate industry became stagnant, and prices fell, and no one consulted it. In the past, it turned mud into gold, but today it turns into... [missing text in original]. The law is changed, and new valuations of real estate are revised so that they can still circulate in the market; [missing text in original]... the burden of industrial and commercial households, and restore the prosperity of the market. (3) Gold... [missing text in original] lending is a matter of course. However, in the financial industry itself, a spirit of mutual assistance should be shown, with mutual exchange of resources and mutual compensation for surpluses and deficits. Maintaining credit among colleagues is the key to securing one's own business strategy. In cooperation with industry and commerce, sincere cooperation should be sought. Industrial and commercial enterprises should provide the financial industry with their internal realities. The financial industry should also proceed from the major premise of supporting the development of industry and commerce and national interests. Regardless of the size of the enterprise, it should only ask whether the enterprise is important, whether it is promising, and whether the inflexibility of turnover is a temporary phenomenon, and whether the sluggishness of business is the trend of the times. It may formulate improvement strategies for it, or point out its gains and losses, or grant it overdrafts and renewals, or provide it with appropriate funds, so as not to be constrained by narrow and cautious lending. However, we should also be mindful of the difficulties of the financial industry itself, because it is easy to lend money but difficult to recover it. On the one hand, deposits are waiting to be paid, and on the other hand, loans are difficult to recover. If a run on deposits occurs at maturity, it will affect the overall situation with a single hair. Therefore, we hope that the financial industry will support industry and commerce, and we also hope that large depositors will support the national financial industry, so as not to put the national economy in a desperate situation and turn it into an economic aggressor, increasing its momentum. (4) Suppress market rumors to pacify people's hearts. How can market rumors be eliminated? Eliminate the rumors that are like rumors. Rumors are born from speculation, association, pseudo-observations, and facts that are brewing. However, if we can meet each other with sincerity, "words will be believed by the people, and actions will be pleasing to the people," then not only can rumors be quelled, but everything can be done. Someone may say that in today's world, scheming is used, and power is valued. Talking about sincerity in the market is simply not knowing the times. This is true. But if you ask someone in the industrial and commercial sector how to trade, they will answer directly, "Trade with integrity and trustworthiness." Integrity is sincerity. Without sincerity, how can there be trust? How can there be righteousness? Therefore, the problem today is that we cannot trust each other and meet each other with sincerity. If we can be sincere and trustworthy, then we will naturally be stable.

Observing Paper Money from Various Chinese Banks After the Silver Tax 191

— Wu Xiaochen

It is shameful to say that my great China, unable to control its environment, is instead controlled by it, becoming a weak victim. Since countries with the gold standard, such as Britain and Japan, felt the different advantages and disadvantages of currency contraction and expansion and sought their own ways out, they successively abandoned the gold standard. Before long, the United States also adopted the same policy, abandoning the gold standard and further buying silver abroad, causing silver prices to suddenly rise. However, China is a country that uses silver, and after the price of silver increased, the value of Chinese currency increased accordingly, and prices also fell, creating an unparalleled opportunity for various countries to expand their trade with China. However, China's exports suffered significant obstacles due to the daily rise of silver currency exchange rates against other countries' currencies, resulting in even more imports exceeding exports. The outflow of silver will undoubtedly continue to increase, which will inevitably affect China's currency reserves, and may even endanger their stability!

Since the outflow of silver is extremely serious, there must be urgent policies to curb it. Therefore, the financial authorities took decisive measures to implement silver export taxes. Its purpose is obviously to prevent the export of silver, which can also be said to be a method of prohibition through taxation. However, the intention is to lower the domestic silver price, so that it is divorced from the foreign silver price. The domestic silver price will not rise sharply with the foreign silver price, and China's price level will not fall due to the rise of the foreign silver price. This is a temporary emergency and a unilateral remedy, which is extremely beneficial to the export of Chinese goods, and can indirectly prevent the import of foreign goods, which is also a way to reduce the excess of imports over exports. That being said, after the silver tax was levied, the difference between domestic and foreign silver prices became more disparate, leading to the fact of smuggling silver out of the country. Although it has attracted the attention of the authorities and the public, it is known that China's customs anti-smuggling organization is immature, and the markets in Hong Kong and Dalian are closely linked to the mainland. Foreign merchant ships are also protected by consular jurisdiction, so smuggling methods are ingenious and difficult to prevent: one way is to use transit, and the other is to use smuggling. More use is made of the convenience that Central Bank notes can be cashed everywhere, regarding them as a medium for exporting silver. A large amount of Central Bank notes are collected in Shanghai and taken to Tianjin and Beiping for cashing, after which they can be transported out of the country through various passes of the Great Wall, and then transported to foreign countries via Dalian or other ports. Therefore, Central Bank notes in the market once had a premium, and the premium of Yuan coins was even more alarming, reaching 90 yuan per 10,000. It can be seen that there are indeed many unscrupulous profiteers. It is certainly not easy to ban smuggling due to factual limitations, but the public is therefore full of rumors, such as nationalizing silver, implementing inconvertible paper money, etc. Most of them are speculations by speculators, which this article dares not discuss. However, if silver leaks out without any control, using limited legal tender to supply the insatiable outflow is a major event that no one can deny! It is very likely to affect China's currency fund. Therefore, the situation of various Chinese banks issuing paper money is worth observing in the current tense situation of the silver issue.

The history of formal paper money issuance by banks in our country is still short. After the opening of the Commercial Bank of China in the 23rd year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty, it began to issue banknotes in imitation of foreign banks' exchange certificates, which was the beginning of Chinese banks issuing banknotes. Later, the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications followed suit. However, at first, the public's belief in banknotes was minimal, and the ability to circulate was far less extensive than it is today. I still remember that before the tenth year of the Republic of China, in the larger county towns in the interior, silver dollars and banknotes still had to be entered into accounts at different levels. Therefore, in the year before the founding of the Republic of China, the amount of exchange certificates issued by the Shanghai branch of the Bank of China was only more than 755,000 yuan, which shows that the circulation of paper money was very limited in the past. The competition from foreign banks' exchange certificates was also one of the reasons why it was difficult to promote Chinese banks' paper money. After the May 30th Massacre, the Chinese people felt the terror of imperialist economic aggression and refused to use foreign banknotes. Except in treaty ports, where there were no significant results under the threat of foreign force, the exchange certificates of foreign banks in the interior gradually disappeared, creating an opportunity for the promotion of Chinese banks' paper money, which was also the beginning of the increase in the amount of paper money issued by Chinese banks. At that time, the public's trust in paper money also underwent a major change due to the passage of time.

The system of issuing paper money varies from country to country. Although our country's financial authorities did not initially know that foreign banks issuing paper money would lose national sovereignty and impose restrictions, they strongly advocated the unification of domestic bank paper money. The single issuance system was adopted, that is, the right to issue paper money was exclusively enjoyed by the Central Bank. Therefore, in the fourth year of the Republic of China, the former government promulgated five articles of regulations to ban paper money. However, the chaos in our country's financial system is undeniable, and due to political relations, it has in fact changed from a nominally single issuance system to a multiple issuance system. In addition to the Central Bank, other banks, with the permission of the government, can also obtain the right to issue paper money, and this trend has continued to the present. The so-called Central Bank at that time referred to the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications, which managed the national treasury. Now, in addition to the Central Bank, there are ten banks, namely, the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the China-South Bank, the China Industrial Bank, the Commercial Bank of China, the Sze Ming Bank, the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, the Reclamation Bank, the Agricultural and Industrial Bank, and the Agricultural and Commercial Bank, which are all banks specially authorized by the government to issue paper money. Among them, the China-South Bank, after obtaining the right to issue paper money, re-affiliated with the Kincheng Banking Corporation, the Continental Bank, and the Yien Yieh Commercial Bank, adopting a joint reserve issuance system, jointly organizing the Four Banks Reserve Treasury, which became a mutually supportive issuance system. In addition to the above, there is also the indirect issuance certificate system created in the early years of the Republic of China, which is unique to various countries. At the beginning of the creation, the original intention was to enable the banks that directly issued exchange certificates to have the amount of circulation greatly increased due to the promotion of the indirectly issued certificate banks. Other banks with weaker strength would find it more difficult to issue on their own, and the opportunity to get involved would be reduced. Moreover, after the implementation of the certificate system, banks that had not obtained the right to issue paper money, since they had the opportunity to issue indirectly, did not need to rush to seek the right to issue paper money. Therefore, the creation of the certificate system was a legitimate remedy under the advocacy of the single issuance system because it could not avoid the multiple issuance system.

Chinese banks' paper money has gained considerable trust in society today, but the increase or decrease in the number of issues changes with the ebb and flow of the economic situation. Moreover, due to the difference in financial seasons, there will inevitably be a large difference. However, after looking at the total amount of paper money issued by various Chinese commercial banks in Shanghai recently, I feel that the expansion of promotion ability has made great progress in the recent short term.

(Unit: Yuan)

Central Bank 89,034,250

Bank of China 136,868,530

Bank of Communications 57,883,500

Four Banks Reserve Treasury 32,070,473

China Industrial Bank 33,645,413

Commercial Bank of China 24,302,900

Sze Ming Bank 18,310,300

Zhejiang Industrial Bank 9,247,838

Reclamation Bank 7,084,000

Agricultural and Industrial Bank 6,167,262

Agricultural and Commercial Bank …………

Excluding the missing figures for the Agricultural and Commercial Bank, the total number of issues in the above table reached more than 410 million yuan. The Central Bank has made the fastest progress. In the 17th year of the Republic of China, it was only more than 11 million yuan, which is more than seven times the current amount. In the inspection report of the bank in January of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, it was still only more than 46 million yuan, which is also twice as much as today. According to the report of the first inspection of the Bank of China in April of the 17th year of the Republic of China, the amount of issuance was 90 million yuan, which has also increased by 50%. Therefore, based on the total number of issues of various banks in the 17th year of the Republic of China, it was only more than 274 million yuan, which has increased by 136 million yuan compared with the recent figures. The reasons for the increase are certainly more than one, but the result of the increase is that the country's cash is concentrated unexpectedly. In recent years, rural areas across the country have been on the verge of bankruptcy. Organizations that have always played a role in regulating rural finance in the interior have lost their ability to control, causing funds in the interior to flow to cities. Moreover, the rampant banditry and heavy thorns everywhere have caused the possibility of cash staying in the interior to suddenly shrink to below zero. These are all the reasons for the concentration of cash as a whole, which is also a major driving force for the promotion of paper money in recent years. Therefore, the concentration of cash has opened up the situation of paper money replacing legal tender. As for the advantages and disadvantages of the entire national economy, because the effects are different, it is impossible to generalize.

The regulations on paper money reserves are that cash reserves must be at least 60% and guarantee reserves must be at most 40%. Cash reserves are limited to cash and raw gold and silver. Government-issued securities, real estate, and even short-term reliable commercial paper can all be used as guarantee reserves. The purpose of issuing paper money is to use 60% of cash to use 100% of paper money, and invisibly obtain 40% of the issuance amount due to the unprofitable nature of guarantee reserves. However, during the abolition of taels and the adoption of yuan, the Shanghai money shop industry once unofficially unanimously advocated that the 60% cash reserve must be fully paid. It can be seen that the so-called minimum 60% cash reserve was not always fully implemented in the past, so wouldn't the benefit of issuing paper money be even greater! When the certificate system was first implemented, the regulations on reserves were not as strict as they are now. In the fourth year of the Republic of China, the Zhejiang Industrial Bank signed a certificate contract with the Bank of China, setting a record for the Chinese paper money certificate system. According to the certificate regulations set by the Bank of China, anyone who receives exchange certificates from the Bank of China must have 70% cash and 30% securities before they can receive 100% of the banknotes. However, in fact, this regulation was not uniform. For example, Zhejiang Industrial Bank only used 50% cash, 15% securities, and 25% short-term bills, and the Bank of China still had to pay interest on the cash provided to the Zhejiang Industrial Bank. It can be seen that there was no fixed legal percentage for paper money reserves at that time. However, later, certificate banks sprang up one after another, and the Bank of China also slightly changed the certificate regulations, changing the cash from 50% to 60%, securities or real estate remained at 30%, and another 10% was added for short-term bills, which could be cashed at any time if necessary. The current certificate regulations are generally adopted by various banks according to this principle. However, each certificate bank has the obligation to suspend cashing when the bank issuing paper money experiences a run, which provides strong protection for the bank directly issuing paper money to cope with any turmoil, and can also be said to be a kind of guarantee given by the certificate banks.

Since the trend of certificate issuance has been opened and the effect has gradually become apparent, the number of banks requesting certificates from banks directly issuing paper money has increased year by year. Until recently, almost every bank that has not obtained the right to issue paper money and money shops with wider operations have obtained certificates, and at the same time, they recognize certificate issuance as a unique business item. In the past six or seven years, the promotion of paper money has been so rapid, which is also one of the reasons. However, whether it is a directly issuing bank or an indirectly issuing certificate bank, they must put the paper money into circulation, hoping that it will circulate in society, and the longer it lasts, the more profitable it will be. Of course, they hope that customers will use it for the method of putting paper money into circulation. However, there are currently eleven banks issuing paper money in Shanghai alone, and certificate banks are everywhere, so the competition is extremely fierce. Considering what customers want, the supply is far from enough. If paper money cannot be put into circulation, not only will there be no profit, but also interest losses will have to be borne. Therefore, they try every possible means to put it into circulation at any time and anywhere. All large-scale factories distribute wages, and huge amounts of money are used to purchase agricultural products from the interior, all of which can spread huge amounts of money to the general public in one day. The wider the scope of distribution, the slower the time it takes for the distributed paper money to return to the bank. Therefore, these occasions where money is needed are also generally recognized as the most suitable places for promoting paper money. Therefore, if commercial and industrial organizations in Shanghai and larger stores need banknotes, they can notify the bank or certificate bank by telephone, instructing them to send the banknotes, and only need to exchange them for a money shop draft with a later date. In addition, the bank or certificate bank subsidizes the store a handling fee of 6 yuan per 10,000 yuan. Even regular customers can usually pay their bills seven days later when using banknotes. More superior stores can have a ten-day cycle, but the minimum amount used is 1,000 yuan. In recent years, many small money shops have carried banknotes with letterheads to the interior to exchange them with various money shops, and the small money shops separately pay the exchange fee. In this way, the infighting between banknotes is inevitable, and the opposition that gradually forms is incompatible. Therefore, the dispute between each other is becoming more and more intense, and the benefits of banknotes are becoming more and more marginal. At present, it is almost stepping into another situation of mutual killing!

The circulation of paper money has such unreasonable phenomena as described above. However, the creation of the certificate system was originally a remedy for the inevitable multiple issuance under the advocacy of single issuance. Now it has instead formed a competition among multiple parties, so it is obvious that this paper money is not really needed by society. Today, when the number of bank issues has increased sharply, there is also an unavoidable question of exaggeration. Since the silver tax was levied, society has been worried about the increase in smuggling. The foreign exchange rate has suddenly increased, and the result of the outflow of silver and goods has made the silver base extremely tight. Therefore, at the end of the year, various money shops in Shanghai experienced a major storm. Now, at the beginning of the early spring when various industries have not yet started, the foreign exchange rate is high, so the opportunity for paper money to stay in society is suddenly reduced, which will inevitably speed up the rate of return to the bank. Moreover, paper money cannot be used in conjunction with spot goods according to the promotion methods previously adopted by various banks. After the silver tax is levied, the price of silver changes into two types: Chinese and world. At this moment, when it is impossible to ban the export of smuggled silver, the price of silver coins and paper money will be more disparate, and the premium of Yuan coins can be used as clear evidence. The sudden increase in the cashing of paper money is therefore inevitable. The recent serious situations such as the freezing of funds and the run on banknotes can be said to have originated from this. If we further investigate the current issuance amount of paper money in Shanghai, which is more than 410 million yuan, according to the legal 60% cash reserve, there are currently about 250 million yuan of silver and goods in Shanghai. Although this reserve is independent, its effect cannot be regarded as a reserve fund for short-term deposits and savings deposits between banks. According to the statistics of various savings banks in Shanghai last year, the savings deposits alone amounted to more than 328 million yuan, which is much larger than the current cash reserve of paper money. Therefore, a large increase in the amount of silver and goods in Shanghai is needed, and the result of the cashing of banknotes not only has the possibility of causing funds to flee, but also gives a strong blow to the indirect preparation of savings deposits. Therefore, the original intention of issuing paper money is nothing more than to save the cost of precious metals, smooth the sluggishness of finance, and relieve the shortage of legal tender. Now, due to the influence of the high price of silver abroad, the inherent center of gravity of paper money has been lost. Of course, we urgently need effective relief. The way to do this now is: on the one hand, we can only imitate the method of jointly establishing a public treasury by various banks set by the Northern Government in the eighth year of the Republic of China, and quickly establish a public treasury by the Bankers' Association in important ports such as Beijing, Shanghai, Tianjin, and Hankou, and make the preparations public to show great trust. Then, on the one hand, limit the cashing of paper money, so that the smuggling of silver and goods will be naturally prohibited. If the transportation of silver is not prohibited, the silver base in the market will become less and less. Since the paper money reserve is based on silver and goods as the mainstream, if the silver base is small, the circulation of paper money will inevitably shrink due to it, and it will not be possible to expand it again for a while. Then, there will be less and less bargaining chips in the market, and the power of the financial community to lend money will naturally shrink accordingly. Therefore, the resulting result is to lower prices, raise interest rates, and the entire national economy may feel threatened at the same time. Then! Establishing a public treasury invisibly unifies the issuance, and then limiting the cashing of paper money, isn't it the key to opening up the current crisis of the outflow of silver and goods and protecting the stability of currency reserves? However, recently there have been rumors in the market that Chinese businessmen have lost 50 million yuan of gold in the trading of American stocks. At this moment, China is thirsty for financial stability. The financial authorities should strictly ban all speculative organizations that are enough to shake China's currency fund.

The Origin of the Financial Industry Panic 192

— Zhu Guangzhao

Characteristics of China's Economic Panic — The severity of China's economic panic has the following characteristics:

(1) Imperialism Shifting Panic to China — Imperialism promotes the sale of surplus cheap goods to China, making it impossible for China's nascent national industries to resist, leading to their collapse.

(2) Shrinking Foreign Markets — Capitalist countries are experiencing their own panic, erecting tariff barriers, and China's exports have plummeted. It is unable to compete in foreign markets, resulting in huge deficits in international payments every year.

(3) Outflow of Silver — In addition to using silver to offset trade deficits, since capitalist countries abandoned the gold standard, they have further increased the price of silver to increase China's purchasing power and buy silver, causing the outflow of silver. This puts China's finances in extreme chaos, and the countryside is again falling into stark bankruptcy?

The Position of Banks in Society — Banks are social financial circulation organs, using funds to invest in industry and commerce to increase circulation speed and expand production. However, the economic panic caused by the imbalance between capitalist production and consumption has shaken the foundations of banks. The collapse of various industrial sectors has implicated banks, leading to the same fate of frequent bankruptcies. The purpose of this article is to reveal the stagnation of China's industry and commerce and the impact of various factors, and to explain the reasons for the collapse of clearing houses:

Stagnation of Industry and Commerce — According to the annual national industrial and commercial conditions published by the International Trade Bureau in the 23rd year, the general situation is as follows:

(1) Cotton Textile Industry — The number of spindles stopped reached 1,224,267, and the average stoppage time was 1-83 hours. The reason is expensive cotton and cheap yarn. Since this year, on the one hand, the supply of cotton is insufficient, and at the same time, American cotton has also risen in price. On the other hand, yarn prices have been greatly reduced due to sluggish sales of existing yarn. The difference between cotton and cotton yarn has formed a scissor-shaped difference, causing the yarn industry to be on the verge of collapse. On the one hand, it is also subject to the pressure of Japanese yarn factories, which is also a particularly important reason.

(2) Withering of the Silk Industry — In the 23rd year, the quantity of raw silk exported from my country decreased greatly. From January to October, exports were only 26,170 metric tons, worth 18,043,752 yuan, a decrease of 33% compared with the same period last year, and a decrease in value of 56%. According to the Shishi Xinbao on January 21 this year, after the sharp reduction in silk exports, factories in various places were unable to maintain operations and were almost completely shut down. Taking Shanghai as an example, only 11 factories are barely operating. The most prosperous time was 117 factories, which is now less than one-tenth.

(3) Flour Industry — Since the loss of the Northeast, my country's flour industry has been in dire straits almost every day. Not only was there no turnaround in the 23rd year, but the situation worsened, especially in the first half of the year. Due to overproduction and falling market conditions, it was difficult for various factories to maintain operations, and they successively stopped or reduced production. After June, due to lack of rain, the purchase volume in the interior increased, and the problem of the Ping-Shen Railway being open to traffic was resolved, and the sales of flour in North China turned prosperous, and the flour market turned around. In early October, the downward trend intensified again, and the flour market returned to the depressed state of the first half of the year. However, the large reduction in foreign flour imports this year is a special phenomenon, due to my country's increased import tax on wheat flour and the weak purchasing power of the people in the interior.

(4) Tea Market — More stable. A total of 428,367 piculs of tea leaves were exported, an increase of 18% compared with the same period last year, worth 31,842,683 national currency, an increase of about 8% compared with last year.

(5) Cement and Matches — From January to June, 246,027,280 kilograms of cement were produced, a decrease of 2% compared with the same period last year, while sales increased. The production and sales of matches both shrank, with production decreasing by about 20% compared with the same period last year, and sales decreasing by about 18%. The reasons for the shrinkage are roughly: 1. Increased consolidated tax, increased costs; 2. Increased tax evasion, reduced prices; 3. There are still many foreign matches imported, especially the increased production of foreign-owned match factories in China, which has put great pressure on Chinese merchants.

(6) Coal and Rubber — In the past, my country used one-fourth of its coal and had to rely on foreign coal supply. After the Ministry of Finance revised and increased import tax rates, the cost of foreign coal increased and shipments to China decreased, and coal prices also fell. The operating conditions of rubber factories have declined in terms of production, sales are sluggish, and coupled with competition from the same industry and foreign goods, market prices have repeatedly fallen.

Repercussions of the U.S. Silver Purchasing Policy — Since the United States implemented an inflationary policy, it has raised the price of silver and bought silver, resulting in a continuous outflow of silver from China. According to last year's customs statistics, the total amount of silver exported was more than 280 million yuan. The money supply is tight, and the financial industry is fundamentally shaken. The most obvious example is that more than 20 silver firms in Shantou closed down last year because they could not cash out due to the outflow of silver. According to the Hong Kong Industrial and Commercial Daily on November 7: "It is found that silver merchants in Shantou have purchased millions of yuan of silver from Shanghai in recent days to import, and they have the intention to maintain finance, and it is more than enough to handle the cash redemption of guaranteed banknotes. However, these people do not do this. All the imported silver dollars are stored, and the financial market is as dry as before. The Hong Kong exchange rate has soared in recent days, and unscrupulous silver merchants have even transported silver to Hong Kong privately (a profit of 100 to 200 yuan can be made for every 1,000 yuan). Each time, the larger amounts reach more than 100,000, although they have been repeatedly seized and confiscated, they still rush to it like water flows downward, and they still risk the law and smuggle as before." Last year, in order to prevent the outflow of silver, the Ministry of Finance increased the silver export tax and levied a balancing tax, but silver continued to flow out. The interbank lending rate has risen to 60%. According to the China News Extra on the 2nd of this month, a telegram from Washington stated: "The silver purchase policy has disrupted China's finances, and officials have expressed regret." "The U.S. government feels powerless to help China's financial crisis. Officials here are well aware of the financial situation in Shanghai and express regret for the plight of China's major commercial ports, saying that the United States has no choice but to abide by its previous commitments to avoid disrupting China's finances with the silver purchase plan. ... " Recently, the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications have stated that they have purchased 20 million yuan of silver and specially released large sums of money to maintain the market during the old New Year, which seems to be able to safely get through the New Year. However, even money houses, which have always been known for their stability, have gone bankrupt in as many as four cases, and major banks have also experienced bank runs. They can only ease the atmosphere for a while, and there are countless crises lurking.

Unsoundness of the Organization Itself — Last year, 13 new banks were established in Shanghai alone, and 7 were closed (this year there is also the Tongyi Bank). According to the conversation of Lin Kanghou, the secretary-general of the Bankers' Association, recorded in the Shishi Xinbao on January 23, he said: "In recent years, the banking industry in this city has been slightly inferior due to the bankruptcy of the rural areas in the interior. In addition, last year, the interior was barren, and it was affected by the U.S. silver policy, resulting in a strange tightness of silver. Small banks with generally unsound organizations and insufficient strength will be stranded and closed or suspended even if they are occasionally unable to turn around." It is estimated that those who closed or went bankrupt last year were: China Industrial Development, Shanghai Overseas Chinese Trust Company, Wuhua Bank, Shanghai Oriental Trust Company, Jiande Bank, Yongan Silver Company, and Huadong Commercial Bank. In particular, the sensational Yongan Silver Company, registered with the Chinese government and filed with the U.S. government, has a magnificent scale, but only less than 200,000 of the 1 million capital was collected, resulting in its inability to turn around and stranding.

Abnormal Development — The bankruptcy of rural areas in the interior and the warlords' melee resulted in cash being concentrated in cities. (For example, the Sichuan warlords' remittances to Shanghai recently rose to 1,700 yuan.) Therefore, banks sprang up like mushrooms after rain, but they suffered from a lack of funds and no way out. In the midst of industrial stagnation, banks mostly adopted a tight policy and did not dare to invest in industry and commerce. They could only take the path of speculation, such as bidding on gold public bonds, which almost became the main business of general banks, which further promoted the great crisis of the banking industry. The most obvious example is the bankruptcy of the Oriental Trust Company, which was completely due to failure in the speculative bidding market. Even the most stable investment, such as real estate, is not reliable. The Tongyi Bank is said to have closed down due to its inability to turn around in real estate investment. The Qianye Association members of the old Guanyuan Character Brand money houses, with strong capital, have closed down in as many as four cases. According to reports, some of them have always made more real estate mortgages. Due to the economic depression, it is difficult to recover the loans, and they have declared liquidation. Therefore, not only is the speculative bidding public bond business not reliable, but also investing in real estate has put banks in misfortune.

In summary, we can see several points, the reasons for the collapse of banks, and at the same time, we understand the current stage of capitalism—from industrial capitalism to financial capitalism—the social relations of production are shackled, and the productive forces are bound to fall into a general collapse.

Advocate Imitating Foreign National Products 198

— Zhou Xian

National goods year, using national goods, this is the most popular. But after "National Goods Year", "Women's National Goods Year", and "Students' National Goods Year", if there is no more national goods year and everyone is happy to use national goods, that is even more popular.

Speaking of national goods, the problem comes. Native cloth with very coarse and short fibers and simple weaving and dyeing methods is naturally a completely authentic national product. However, recently many farmers have been planting fine and long American cotton. This kind of high-quality cotton wool is used by yarn factories and dyeing and weaving factories opened by Chinese people. The cotton cloth produced is completely similar to imported products. The raw materials for this kind of cotton textile are national goods, the manufacturers are factories opened by Chinese people, and the labor is provided by Chinese people. Although the form is imitation of imported products, this is a completely authentic national product. — I think this kind of improved national product should be vigorously promoted and adopted by everyone. It should never be regarded as a foreign product and destroy the lifeline of improved national products just because it imitates foreign products.

To put it more clearly. For example, a suit. A suit is naturally Western-style, but if it is made of national wool fabrics, I think it should also be promoted. It should never be rejected just because the suit is not Chinese-style. There are many other examples, too numerous to mention. I hope that the gentlemen and ladies who advocate national goods will pay attention to this point. If all commodities that do not preserve the antique style are regarded as non-national goods, then to maintain the status of national goods, they must be as unchangeable as a two-cent zongzi candy, wouldn't that be terrible?

A Primary School Student's Cry 199

— Chi Fo

This time I went to the countryside and heard a primary school student crying, which was really sad and moving. Therefore, I have many feelings about "primary school education".

My neighbor, Rongsheng, is ten years old and studies at a ×× primary school in the county. He is smart and lively and can be said to be a top student in the third grade; therefore, every teacher likes him. However, Rongsheng's father is a primary school teacher with a monthly salary of less than 30 yuan. He already feels exhausted trying to support his wife and three sons and two daughters; naturally, there will be problems with the education expenses of his children. Therefore, Rongsheng has been studying at school for five months, and the tuition has not been paid off. The teacher urged him several times, and Rongsheng cried several times in front of his parents; there was really no way, but there was a quarrel in the family.

Last year, during the lunar New Year, Ronger brought a bill back from school. His father saw on the bill: Tuition fee 5 yuan Book fee 1.2 jiao Lecture notes fee 0.6 jiao Tea bag 0.4 jiao Uniform fee 2.4 jiao Craft paper 0.3 jiao Registration fee for the 24th year 1 yuan Total 10.9 jiao

Rongsheng handed the bill to his father and said: The teacher said that if the tuition fee is not paid this time, I will be expelled. As he spoke, tears fell. His father stared at the bill, only dazed, and had nothing else to say. Rongsheng cried, crying very miserably. When I heard such a miserable and sad cry from a child, I felt very sad in my heart, and when I touched my shy pocket, I could only sigh!

Chapter 23: The Return Journey

After the Empress Dowager's planned trip to Changbai Mountain was canceled by the two officials from the Imperial Astronomical Observatory, a strange illusion filled our minds. This illusion had terrible consequences. Even those who were usually calm and collected gradually became agitated and restless. Some even became timid and fearful, like criminals suffering from a guilty conscience. From morning till night, everyone trembled with fear, hoping to return to Beijing as soon as possible. Wine is the Joy of the Immortals 202

— Master Chunyu Lou

Friends who enjoy drinking naturally know that the pleasure in wine is endless. Like the wine immortal Li Bai, who sang in a tavern:

"Three cups lead to the great Dao, a斗 (dou, measurement) unites with nature; just get the fun in wine, don't tell the sober ones."

When Li Guinian heard this song, he said, "This must be Scholar Li!" He hurried upstairs and found Li Bai completely drunk. Guinian stepped forward and said, "The Emperor is waiting at the Agarwood Pavilion! Scholar, go quickly!" Li Bai didn't respond but opened his drunken eyes and recited a poem by Yuanming to Li Guinian: "I am drunk and want to sleep, please go."

After reciting, he fell asleep. Helpless, Li Guinian ordered servants to help him onto a white horse. The crowd helped him all the way to the Five Phoenix Tower. The Emperor then ordered eunuchs to urge him to ride into the palace until he reached the Agarwood Pavilion. The Emperor saw him on horseback with his eyes closed, still not awake. He ordered eunuchs to spread a purple carpet next to the pavilion and helped him off the horse to lie down for a while. The Emperor went to see him and saw saliva flowing from Bai's mouth, so he wiped it with his dragon sleeve. Consort Yang said, "I heard that washing the face with cold water can sober one up." So she ordered the eunuchs to fetch water from the pool to wash his face. Bai woke up, saw the Emperor in front of him, and prostrated himself, saying, "Your subject deserves ten thousand deaths." The Emperor raised him up with his own hand and said, "Today, I am admiring famous flowers with the Consort. We cannot be without new lyrics. Summon the scholar to compose three chapters of Qingping Melody." Bai saw that the writing instruments were all there, so he composed it while drunk in one stroke.

It can be seen that for those who are good at drinking, wine can also help literary inspiration. Those who are not good at drinking naturally do not know the joy of it. Therefore, modern wanderers often use wine to relieve sorrow, which can be described as "one drunk and all things are over." Indeed, wine is the joy of the immortals. Friends who are shrouded in clouds of sorrow, drink as much as you can!

Random Talk

Talking About Various Past Costumes 204

— Zhang Feng

Although new and improved forms often have a retro feel, clothing, which is used to keep warm and adorn the body, has undergone countless ingenious designs and inventions by predecessors. Sometimes, ignoring the rule that "if the clothes do not fit properly, there will be disaster," it has its own special charm in the past that is worth talking about.

Jie Shan (Pieced Robe)…This is a long robe made by joining two different fabrics of two different colors near the waist. The material can be different, as long as they are similar. For example, the upper half is crepe, the lower half is spun silk, the upper half has large flowers, and the lower half has small flowers or no flowers. The value of the materials and the coordination of colors are the conditions for a beautiful jie shan. In the past, upper-class people valued the magua (mandarin jacket) more than people do now. Adding a magua to a long robe was considered a sign of respect and solemnity. People who went out or visited guests mostly wore a magua, covering the upper half of the jie shan, so the material of the upper half of the jie shan could be a little more casual.

Tao Ku (Over-pants)…This is a pair of custom-made trouser legs with no crotch or waistband, used to be worn over pants. The function of the tao ku is twofold: to increase warmth in the lower body and to add beauty, while using less valuable material. Its lower section is the same as ordinary trouser legs, and the upper section is cut into an oblique angle at the knee bend, lower in the back and higher in the front - the lower back is for ease of bending the knees and legs when moving, and the higher front is so that the tips of the high part can be affixed with two straps for attachment to the belt. Tao ku can be single-layered, lined, or cotton-padded. Many men in Jiangnan have them, and in Jiangbei, they are used by both men and women. As times advance, the youths of Jiangnan generously give this thing to the elderly as their patent!

Jia Xiu (False Sleeves), Chen Ling (False Collar)…There are two types of false sleeves: one is a single-layered lining attached to the cuffs of short or long shirts to protect the original sleeves from getting dirty or torn, incidentally making people suspect that it is the cuff of another piece of clothing; the other is an independent sleeve that is not as long as the elbow, made of valuable material, and its sole purpose is to show off wealth, forming "the divine dragon sees its head but not its tail." There are also those made of coarse material with lining or cotton padding, which is very practical for keeping warm, but inevitably shows people that there is one more piece of clothing inside. The latter type of false sleeve has a row of buttons near the opening to prevent it from falling off, defeating its purpose. The chen ling (false collar) has the same function as the false sleeves, with a little more material under the collar, folded together in a pointed shape in front of the chest, and also fitted with a row of buttons. These two small items are worn by brokers when they go to visit guests.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

From the Strange Incident at Tangqiao to Breaking Superstition 205

— Meng Ruo

Recently, a ridiculous and outrageous incident occurred in Tangqiao, Hedong. A group of local ruffians, in order to promote a temple fair in the countryside, went to the Tiantian Temple in the eastern town of the village on the night of the Lantern Festival and carried out the small statue of the Zhaotianhou deity enshrined in the temple. A large crowd quickly gathered and went to a nearby public cemetery to perform "pao tan" (running the altar) and "jiao tang" (calling the hall). They cracked open the coffins of newly deceased unclaimed bodies on the tombs and forcibly removed the dead people's heads, hanging them on the chair of the small deity. It is said that they held the same event again the night before.

This behavior of the ignorant and foolish people of Tangqiao is certainly bizarre and inhumane. However, the behaviors that contributed to this bizarre and inhumane act are of a superstitious mindset. Therefore, we cannot just look at it as bizarre or inhumane.

The superstitious minds of the Chinese villagers are still deeply rooted, influenced by historical traditional thoughts. For example, the reason why the villagers hold temple fairs is not simply for the sake of having fun, but because they believe that holding temple fairs will bring peace to the area. We only need to look at a village holding a temple fair when there is a bad harvest or an epidemic to understand their purpose for holding the temple fair. The meaning of the Tangqiao event is undoubtedly the same. It's just that their actions are slightly bizarre and inhumane.

Eliminating the superstitious minds of the Chinese people cannot be achieved simply by slogans or signs like "Down with superstition." Because slogans are equal to empty talk and can at best wake people's ears and eyes for a moment. Even using pressure to prohibit it is futile. Forcing people to get rid of superstition will be like forcing people to switch to the national calendar. People can obey in appearance but disobey in their hearts.

Therefore, the best way to eliminate the superstitious minds of the people is to work hard on education. It must be known that the cultivation of superstition has a long history and cannot be completely eliminated overnight. We should use educational methods to vigorously instill scientific knowledge into the general public, explaining the pros and cons of superstition, so that the people can realize the necessity of eliminating superstition themselves. In this way, the people's superstitious minds will gradually be improved and eliminated.

There is another point that those engaged in breaking superstition must pay attention to. That is, the villagers' holding of temple fairs contains a recreational function in addition to asking for peace and tranquility in the area. Because Chinese villages have always lacked recreational venues. A group of villagers work hard all year round and cannot get a chance to enjoy themselves. For the sake of physical and mental relaxation, they have to take advantage of the temple fairs to have fun for a while. Therefore, if we want the Chinese people to eliminate superstitious minds, we should set up more recreational venues in the villages and hold various exhibitions several times a year, so that the villagers can increase their knowledge and get proper recreational opportunities. In this way, the superstitious behavior of holding temple fairs in the countryside will fall without being overthrown.

Twilight 206

— Qin Jian

This year's spring will no longer have green tones; in the cold rain and snow, it appears with the brown posture of late autumn.

And the world of this spring is also hanging up a gray-yellow curtain.

— Is it the accumulation of the years, or is it the drop in the mercury column on the thermometer? Even in spring, I have the mood of a wilting autumn sunflower.

The tone is one of desolation and indifference. The heart is as barren as a small courtyard in late autumn with fallen leaves dancing.

Even if I have good intentions toward the migratory birds with clipped tails traveling to the south, what I get is still as terrible as a dying candle and the desolation of the Middle Ages on the branches of plum blossoms.

From this, I began to understand that age has pulled people to the edge of an unknowable cave: and people are no longer children suitable for a bright season.

(The world always belongs to the new, the younger generation; and you, who have hung up the dark curtain of twilight, what else is more suitable for you to miss other than some endless late autumn evenings?)

It's really hard to believe even myself: Could it be that the historical facts of a bloody life for many years represent this endless string of late autumn evenings? Ha, God knows where the key to this magic of life lies!

However, a soul that grows in stubbornness will not willingly be dissolved in the unfair twilight. Although in mornings and evenings, people may be occupied by a withered terror, a twilight desolation is vaguely reflected in front of me, like a dream, like smoke. So, I comprehend a small scene of a desert sunset: a group of camels crawling hard, like snails on the damp corners of walls, and the north wind blowing out the cold metallic sound. The travelers ask for grass and clear water, but finally fall horizontally in the endless sea of sand. A gust of wind deeply buries them into the strata—the sun on the horizon is gray and black.

My heart trembled in cold sweat: Did I really have a twilight mood? And I, I grew up in stubbornness!

So, I chose a bright morning, picked up a copy of Schopenhauer's "Studies in Pessimism", grabbed a chair, and sat in the strong sun in the courtyard.

What I hope for is: maybe there will be a young mood as bright as the sun?

The tone of twilight has no reason to grow in the sun.

But, strangely, when the sun shines golden flowers between the pages of the book, the venomous snake of old age that makes people tremble also awakens. The speed of imagery is unimaginable, and at the same time, it cannot be calculated with mathematical equations: in the warm courtyard's sunlight, an old man's loneliness begins to break into the lawn of barren ideas again. I remembered the old man in "Rip Van Winkle".

(Isn't there also so much dreamlike sorrow of old people in the sun of the big meadow?)

The warmth, laughter, blue romance, and brown suffering of the past conjure up seven-colored shadows in the sun. Then tears also float on the wrinkled face, dripping and resting on the trembling pale lips, like ice crystals on withered leaves in winter.

In the burning of tobacco leaves, in the movement of the sun, the tragedy of life appears endlessly once again, and this old man who pursues warmth and moves with the sun, isn't he delightfully regarded as a sundial?

And this sundial not only indicates the time but also indicates the way out of life.

I understand that the sorrow of twilight is pressing on people's hearts, and there is no way to escape it: when life reaches a gray stage, there is no way to disguise it even in the sun!

So I calmed down: the sorrow of twilight is a more stubborn venomous snake than me, which cannot be avoided in the world.

Home 207

— Hua Zhi

Many single friends envy me for having a home, and I used to envy others this way when I was single. Every day, I dragged my tired body back from the office, thinking that my wife would greet me with a smiling face at the door, take off my coat for me, and present me with a freshly brewed cup of Longjing tea. Smoking cigarettes like this, or sharing the candies I brought back: naturally, it is incomparable to the lonely sleep in the center of the bed when I was single. Sometimes, when going out, I made an appointment in advance! As soon as the doorbell rang, my wife, dressed in new clothes, had already jumped in front of me, knowingly took my arm, and rushed to the 5:30 movie. The fatigue of the day was imperceptibly reaped from the wife's charming laughter and whispers. If there is an innocent little baby who throws himself from his wife's arms while learning to speak, and you want him to call out "Dad," that kind of

Page 21

pleasure is enough for single men to envy endlessly.

From envying others, I was envied by others. I spent three years living a "home" life like heaven. There is a charming child running and jumping on the ground, and everything is maintaining the same situation as when the home started, but I feel that home is not as lovely as it used to be! This is naturally incomprehensible to single friends.

A good friend sent a letter from a distant place. He got married. He told me so proudly: From today on, he is a person with a home. My own experience may not be a model for every home. I read that letter with contrary eyes to his overly happy tone. In the reply, I said: Home is heaven. We can get happiness from her that we have never enjoyed before. At the same time, home is also an invisible chain. It makes us suffer from the pain we have never experienced! The old friend who is in honeymoon may be aroused to be dissatisfied. He should be happy at the time he is contentedly with a home he has been yearning for long, but he will gradually understand the reason for this sentence.

The Decline of the Paper Sheep 208

— Taku Ren

Children always look forward to celebrating the New Year and festivals. Whenever there are New Year or festivals, they will happily smile. After eating the tangyuan of the Winter Solstice, they will want to get the "lucky money" of the New Year's Eve, and after the New Year, they will look forward to playing with lanterns on the fifteenth night of the Lantern Festival. Therefore, children are as clear about remembering the New Year and festivals as the housewives in the family.

When I was a child, although my family worshiped Christianity, we were as lively as other families every New Year and festival, with food and fun. Therefore, I still remember some programs clearly. I was especially interested in the Lantern Festival.

The Lantern Festival, according to the customs there, is the liveliest day of the year in all events. Children especially are even happier. Both the county and the countryside perform community operas starting from the twelfth or thirteenth. On the fourteenth, there will be a big celebration of welcoming the gods, which will continue until the seventeenth or eighteenth. Therefore, children can have extra fun during this event.

Children, no matter how poor their families are, all carry or pull many paper carp, paper sheep, paper gold coins, and other paper lanterns on the fourteenth night. The children in a community or village all compete with paper lanterns in groups on this night. Whose is made well, whose is made novel, special, or large, the results will be determined on this night. On the fifteenth night, everyone arranges according to the results of the competition, setting off rockets, firecrackers, and firecrackers, and they will continue to have fun until late at night before going home.

It seems that I was only ten years old at that time. My brother specially made a very large paper sheep for me. The result of the competition on the fourteenth night was the first. The happiness at that time was really more exciting than anything else. The children all called me "Big Brother."

From this year on, I have never been back to my hometown for the Lantern Festival. I have also gradually grown older, and I have lost the interest I had in paper sheep when I was a child.

The last time I returned to my hometown, recalling the childhood situation at that time, I was also happy. On the fifteenth night, I went with my brothers to watch community operas and the lantern festival of the children in each community. This night made me feel disappointed. The community operas were not as lively as before. The children's lantern festival was not as spectacular as it used to be. The welcoming of the gods was also very deserted without much excitement.

It has been three years since I have celebrated the Lantern Festival. If I hadn't seen the children pulling paper sheep tonight, I would have almost forgotten the festival that I used to have the most fun with as a child.

The Lantern Festival used to be such a lively day. It has been the same for thousands of years, but in recent years, it has become a situation of deteriorating day by day, just like the life of me, this wanderer. Just walking into the apartment, seeing the very sparse children pulling paper sheep and setting off firecrackers, I couldn't help but think of the grand occasion of the competition of paper sheep, paper carp, paper gold coins, etc., in my childhood. Although that time was not as good as before, three years ago was not as good as that year, but now, it is even worse than the Lantern Festival night I saw three years ago.

Wandering is wandering day by day, and people are getting older day by day. The scene in front of me is also changing rapidly, and this Lantern Festival is becoming more and more indifferent generation after generation.

Everything is in a recession, and even the Lantern Festival, which is a night without sleep for children, is in a recession. We are considered to have enjoyed the blessing of playing, but it is sad that the children are sinking into a recession year after year.

Three People Walking Together 209

— Mu Yilong

Page 22

Paper sheep, in this era, can only sigh alone at the sorrow of fate.

Whip Marks 210

— Wei Jin

They already quarreled last night. In Xinmin's case, he suffered a bellyful of anger from the outside, thinking that only his wife understood him, and told his wife to calm his anger, but when he came home, his wife opened her mouth and added fuel to the fire, making him even more angry.

His wife said, "Going out for a day and not finding a single penny, it would be better for me to go." He listened to an unknown fire rising ten feet high, "It would be better for you to go? Then why don't you go?" He had never spoken to his wife in such a fierce and loud voice. This time, he broke the rule. His wife couldn't bear it, of course, and felt insulted. The more she thought about it, the more sad she became. Why are you so fierce to me? I only said that one sentence. Can't we talk calmly? His wife began to cry. With crying and speaking, she said, "Why don't I go? …Isn't it because I want to save face for you? Can't I open my mouth to borrow money from people? We've only been married for a short time, and I'm already running around to borrow money from people. Wouldn't people laugh at me? It doesn't matter if I'm ridiculed, it doesn't matter… Where did your face hide? …Why don't I go? Don't I want to go? Have I ever said that I don't want to go? …"

Originally, he was angry, but after his wife cried, it was his wife who was angry instead of him. He felt that he had said too much and shouldn't have. His wife had a reason, and he shouldn't have made his wife feel wronged and sad. He not only didn't get angry but felt ashamed, feeling sorry for his wife. He wanted to change his attitude and explain to his wife in a more gentle manner, but at the same time, he felt that this was not possible—he would give in to her as soon as she cried and made a fuss, and this trend must not be allowed to continue, as the days of cohabitation are still long. However, if he didn't explain to his wife in a gentle manner, his wife would naturally not give in, and this would also make the current situation impossible to resolve. He felt extremely uncomfortable in his heart, and the flames of pain were burning his entire soul.—He took out a cigarette from his pocket, lit it, and smoked it. His mouth was blowing smoke, his eyes staring out the window, and his brows were tightly furrowed. He showed a melancholy expression.

His wife never cried or made a fuss, and this time she also broke the rule. She sat on the bed and cried for a while. Seeing that he didn't talk back but stared out the window to smoke, showing a melancholy expression, she knew that he was not angry but sad. He was angry with me today because he couldn't borrow money. He hadn't been angry before. He must have been angry outside. You gave him anger when he already received other people's anger, aren't you understanding him? You shouldn't give him comfort, and you want to make him angry? …It's really wrong. Now that he is made uncomfortable and melancholy, it is really a sin. His wife was regretting, not crying but sad, she silently watched tears flow.

He smoked for a while, in melancholy and sadness, and suddenly didn't hear his wife's crying and talking. He looked back and saw his wife crying sadly. He felt that he had never been angry with his wife before, and had never made his wife cry sadly. This time, his actions were too cruel. He left the window, ran to the bed, and wanted to explain to his wife, but as soon as he sat down next to his wife, his wife burst into tears and fell into his arms…

Adventure in Difficulty 211

— Xuan

What causes the most suffering for countless young people now is the difficulty in solving the problems of seeking education and seeking employment. Seeking education is the first hurdle, and seeking employment is the second hurdle. The second hurdle is actually even more difficult than the first. Indeed, with the bankruptcy of all industries in our country and a surplus of manpower, young people seeking employment see society as an impenetrable wall, with no way to find an outlet. They often end up on detours they originally did not want to take. This phenomenon makes one deeply feel the seriousness of the situation, which conceals the endless difficulties and dangers in the future of young people.

There are two ways to remedy this serious situation: first, we must use a spirit of great fearlessness to break down the copper wall of society; second, we must work hard to move forward and create new careers for the future. Do not be afraid of difficulties, do not be afraid of dangers, as long as you take the risk, follow the plan, and move forward towards the goal, you can overcome those difficulties and dangers.

So-called adventure seems the same as recklessness, but they are actually different. A reckless person has no goal, no plan, and is like a blind man riding a blind horse, blundering forward in confusion. Adventure is not like that. First, there is a clear goal and a well-thought-out plan, and then one moves forward towards the goal according to the plan. The so-called "danger" refers to the difficulties encountered on the way forward. The so-called adventure means using a spirit of great fearlessness to overcome difficulties in order to implement the plan and achieve the goal. Those who have a goal, a plan, and are not afraid of danger have already clearly known that this goal and this plan require overcoming this difficulty. They only strive to devise ways to cope with it, and have no intention of panicking or retreating. Therefore, there is a lasting spirit of great fearlessness, which is not a temporary emotional impulse, but the result of a rational and insightful understanding.

For those who subscribe to the magazine for the whole year, the domestic postage is 1.5 yuan. All domestic first, second, and third-class post offices can subscribe on behalf of them, which saves remittance fees, postage, and procedures, making it convenient and quick.
